# Muse dev backlog вҖ” the living ledger

- вҳ… RESPONSE-EXPERIENCE (2026-07-12, м§„м•Ҳ м§Ғм ‘ мҡ”мІӯ вҖ” 20m мһҗмңЁлЈЁн”„ `response-experience`мқҳ м „мҡ© нҒҗ; м–ҙмӢңмҠӨн„ҙнҠё мқ‘лӢө кІҪн—ҳмқ„ кі„мҶҚ лҚ” мўӢкІҢ. кё°л°ҳ: мұ„л„җ лҢҖнҷ” лҰ¬л“¬(мһЎлӢҙ fast-pathВ·ліөм°Ҫ ackВ·мқёмҡ© мҷ„лЈҢліҙкі )В·к°ңмһ… мҳҲмӮ°+лӢӨмқҙм ңмҠӨнҠёВ·мӣҗн„°м№ҳ veto, м „л¶Җ main лЁём§ҖлҗЁ):
  - в—Ұ мә”л“ң casual мқ‘лӢө н•ңкөӯм–ҙ нҢЁлҰ¬нӢ° вҖ” `casualResponseFor`(agent-core)к°Җ мҳҒм–ҙ кі м •мқҙлқј н•ңкөӯм–ҙ мқёмӮ¬("м•Ҳл…•~")м—җ мҳҒм–ҙ мә”л“ң мқ‘лӢөмқҙ к°җ; мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ м–ём–ҙ(мһ…л Ҙм—җ н•ңкёҖ мЎҙмһ¬) к°җм§Җн•ҙ KO м№ҙн”ј м…Ӣ м¶”к°Җ, CLI/мұ„л„җ м–‘мӘҪ нҢҢлҰ¬нӢ°, кё°мЎҙ EN н…ҢмҠӨнҠё л¬ҙліҖкІҪ green мң м§Җ.
  - в—Ұ н”„лЎңм•ЎнӢ°лёҢ м•ҢлҰј к·јкұ° н•ң мӨ„ вҖ” pattern/ambient/commitment м•ҢлҰј ліёл¬ём—җ "мҷң м§ҖкёҲ мқҙкұё л§җн•ҳлҠ”м§Җ"(к°җм§Җлҗң нҢЁн„ҙВ·к·ңм№ҷВ·м•ҪмҶҚмқҳ к·јкұ°) лӘ…мӢң; к·јкұ°лҠ” м ҖмһҘлҗң мӮ¬мӢӨмқҳ verbatim/кІ°м •лЎ  мЎ°н•©л§Ң(мғҲ fabrication н‘ңл©ҙ кёҲм§Җ), factSheet/rule лҚ°мқҙн„°м—җм„ң лҸ„м¶ң. лҰ¬м„ңм№ҳ к·јкұ°: к·јкұ° м—ҶлҠ” мҙҲк°ңмқёнҷ”=к°җмӢңк°җ(к°Җм№ҳв‘Ө).
  - в—Ұ мң„мһ„ ack мӨ‘ліө м–өм ң вҖ” мөңмў… м „мҶЎ мӢӨнҢЁвҶ’лӢӨмқҢ нӢұ мһ¬мӢңлҸ„ мӢң ліөм°Ҫ ackк°Җ н•ң лІҲ лҚ” к°ҖлҠ” мҲҳмҡ©лҗң м—Јм§ҖлҘј мӢӨм ңлЎң лӢ«кё°(мҳҲ: inboundлі„ ack-sent л§ҲнӮ№мқ„ handled-нӮӨмҷҖ лі„лҸ„ мӮ¬мқҙл“ңм№ҙлЎң, ackлҠ” 1нҡҢл§Ң).
  - в—Ұ digest лқјмқё injection-span мӨ‘нҷ” кІҖнҶ  вҖ” digest м»ҙнҢҢмқј лқјмқём—җ recap.ts `safeRecapText`лҘҳ мӨ‘нҷ” м Ғмҡ© м—¬л¶Җ кІ°м •+кө¬нҳ„(мҶҢмҠӨ лЈЁн”„ м»ЁлІӨм…ҳкіј мқјкҙҖм„ұ мң м§Җн•ҳл©°; мӢ лў°л¶Ҳк°Җ н…ҚмҠӨнҠёк°Җ нҒҗлҘј нғҖлҠ” кІҪлЎңк°Җ мӢӨмһ¬н•ҳлҠ”м§Җ лЁјм Җ мЎ°мӮ¬).
  - в—Ұ digest-sent cross-process л ҲмқҙмҠӨ мҷ„нҷ” вҖ” api+cli л‘җ лҚ°лӘ¬мқҙ к°ҷмқҖ sent-sidecarлҘј checkвҶ’markн•ҳлҠ” м°Ҫм—җм„ң мӨ‘ліө лӢӨмқҙм ңмҠӨнҠё к°ҖлҠҘ; мӣҗмһҗм Ғ л§ҲнӮ№(mkdir-lock лҳҗлҠ” лӢЁмқј лҚ°лӘ¬ мҶҢмң к¶Ң к·ңм№ҷ)мңјлЎң лӢ«кё°.
  - в—Ұ ack м№ҙн”ј/нҶӨ к°ңм„  вҖ” composeAck н”„лЎ¬н”„нҠёВ·к°Җл“ң нҠңлӢқ(ліөм°Ҫмқҙ лҚ” мһҗм—°мҠӨлҹҪкі  м§§кІҢ, "лӢӨ лҗҳл©ҙ м•Ңл ӨмӨ„кІҢ" мқјкҙҖм„ұ), eval:channel-rhythm мјҖмқҙмҠӨлЎң pin.

- вң“ **channel-veto V1-V3 вҖ” н”„лЎңм•ЎнӢ°лёҢ м•ҢлҰј мӣҗн„°м№ҳ off (мұ„л„җ "к·ёл§Ң" лӢөмһҘ вҶ’ н•ҷмҠө м№Ёл¬ө)** (worktree `channel-veto`): V1 вҖ” `applyInterruptionBudget`(packages/proactivity/interruption-gate.ts)м—җ `avoidedSources`(trust-ledger vetoed мҶҢмҠӨ мҠӨнӮө, send/digest м „л¶Җ м•Ҳ н•Ё) + `lastDeliveryFile`(л§Ҳм§Җл§ү л°°лӢ¬ sourceKey мӮ¬мқҙл“ңм№ҙ) мҳөм…ҳ, 5к°ң unasked лЈЁн”„ + api/cli лҚ°лӘ¬ л°°м„ . V2 вҖ” `apps/api/src/inbound-veto-handler.ts`: мұ„л„җм—җм„ң "к·ёл§Ң"/"stop" лҘҳ **лӢЁлҸ…-л°ңнҷ”**(нҸ¬н•Ё л§Өм№ҳ м•„лӢҳ) лӢөмһҘ + 24h лӮҙ мөңк·ј л°°лӢ¬ кё°лЎқмқҙ мһҲмқ„ л•Ңл§Ң к·ё мҶҢмҠӨлҘј vetoedлЎң кё°лЎқн•ҳкі  нҷ•мқё л©”мӢңм§Җ л°ҳнҷҳ(л¶Ҳм¶©мЎұ/кіөмң мұ—/лҜёнҺҳм–ҙл§Ғ/кё°лЎқмӢӨнҢЁлҠ” м „л¶Җ нҸҙмҠӨлЈЁ, кұ°м§“ нҷ•мқё кёҲм§Җ); `createInboundAgentRun`м—җ approval лӢӨмқҢВ·casual м•һмңјлЎң л°°м„ . V3 вҖ” лҗҳлҸҢлҰ¬кё°лҘј мӢӨм ңлЎң лҸҷмһ‘н•ҳкІҢ: `avoidedSourceKeys`к°Җ мҶҢмҠӨлӢ№ ANY-vetoed-winsмқҙлҚҳ кІғмқ„ **LATEST-OUTCOME-WINS**(outcomeAtMs мҲң, лҸҷлҘ мқҖ нҢҢмқјмҲң)мңјлЎң ліҖкІҪн•ҙ `muse proactive keep <source>`к°Җ м§„м§ң un-vetoк°Җ лҗҳлҸ„лЎқ мҲҳм •(recordOutcomeмқҖ кё°мЎҙм—җлҸ„ лҜёл§Өм№ӯ мӢң appendн•ҳкі  мһҲм–ҙ лі„лҸ„ мҲҳм • л¶Ҳмҡ”, лҢҖм№ӯм„ұ нҷ•мқён•Ё); нҷ•мқё л©”мӢңм§Җк°Җ мӢӨмЎҙ лӘ…л №(`muse proactive keep <source>`)мқ„ м•ҲлӮҙн•ҳлҸ„лЎқ к°ұмӢ ; vetoвҶ’keepвҶ’avoidedSourceKeys мһ¬нҷ•мқёвҶ’мһ¬л°°лӢ¬к№Ңм§Җмқҳ нҶөн•© н…ҢмҠӨнҠё(packages/proactivity/test/interruption-gate.test.ts) + latest-wins мң лӢӣ н…ҢмҠӨнҠё(packages/stores) м¶”к°Җ. FEATURES.md лҠҘлҸҷм„ұ м Ҳ н•ң мӨ„ + мқҙ мӨ„. кІ°м •лЎ  vitest л Ҳмқҙм–ҙлЎң м¶©л¶„ нҢҗлӢЁ(лқјмқҙлёҢ LLM л°°н„°лҰ¬ л¶Ҳн•„мҡ” вҖ” нҢЁн„ҙл§Өм№ӯВ·мӣҗмһҘлЎңм§Ғ м „л¶Җ л№„-лӘЁлҚё). нҸүк°Җмһҗ PASS нӣ„ м»Өл°Ӣ/лЁём§Җ лҢҖкё°.

- вң“ **interruption-budget B1-B3 вҖ” к°ңмһ… мҳҲмӮ° + м Җл…Ғ лӢӨмқҙм ңмҠӨнҠё** (worktree `interruption-budget`): 5к°ң unasked н”„лЎңм•ЎнӢ°лёҢ лЈЁн”„(pattern-firingВ·ambient-noticeВ·followup-firingВ·background-exit-noticeВ·commitment-checkin)мқҳ send м§Ғм „м—җ кІ°м •лЎ  мҳҲмӮ° кІҢмқҙнҠё(`applyInterruptionBudget`, packages/proactivity/interruption-gate.ts вҖ” мҠ¬лқјмқҙл”© мңҲлҸ„ мӢңк°„лӢ№/мқјмқј м№ҙмҡҙнҠё, `withinInterruptionBudget`)лҘј л°°м„ ; мҳҲмӮ° мҙҲкіјл¶„мқҖ dedupe sidecarлҠ” л°°лӢ¬лҗң кІғмІҳлҹј л§ҲнӮ№н•ҳл©ҙм„ң `digest-queue.json`м—җ verbatim м Ғмһ¬(B2, мқҙлҜё м»Өл°Ӣ). B3(мқҙлІҲ мҠ¬лқјмқҙмҠӨ): м Җл…Ғ лӢӨмқҙм ңмҠӨнҠё flush вҖ” `runDigestFlushIfDue`(packages/proactivity/digest-flush.ts, LLM лҜёмӮ¬мҡ©В·мҲңмҲҳ м»ҙнҢҢмқј)к°Җ лЎңм»¬ `MUSE_DIGEST_HOUR`(кё°ліё 18мӢң)м—җ нҒҗ мҠӨлғ…мғ·мқ„ н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ л©”мӢңм§ҖлЎң м»ҙнҢҢмқј(н—ӨлҚ”+"В· [source] HH:MM text"мӨ„, мҳӨлІ„н”ҢлЎңмӢң мөңмӢ н•ӯлӘ© ліҙмЎҙ+"вҖҰand N more" нҠёл Ҳмқјл§Ғ лқјмқё)н•ҙ м „мҶЎ нӣ„ мҠӨлғ…мғ· `upToAt`(м „мІҙ мҠӨлғ…мғ·мқҳ MAX at)к№Ңм§Җл§Ң drain вҖ” м „мҶЎ мӢӨнҢЁмӢң нҒҗ ліҙмЎҙ+sidecar лҜёл§ҲнӮ№, л°ңмҶЎ м„ұкіөмқҖ `digest-sent-store.ts`(лЎңм»¬ мәҳлҰ°лҚ”-мқј sidecar)лЎң н•ҳлЈЁ 1нҡҢ dedupe. apps/api `digest-tick.ts`(proactive-tickкіј лҸҷмқј мұ„л„җ/мһҗкІ©, `MUSE_DIGEST_ENABLED` кё°ліё true)мҷҖ apps/cli `commands-daemon-register.ts`(к°ҷмқҖ mirroring, CLI м „мҡ© лЈЁн”„мқҳ digestлҸ„ flush) м–‘мӘҪ лҚ°лӘ¬м—җ л°°м„ . мқҪкё° м „мҡ© `muse digest list`(--json, лӢӨмқҢ flush нһҢнҠё) мӢ к·ң лӘ…л №. л“ңлқјмқҙлёҢл°”мқҙ мҲҳм •: `pattern-firing-loop.ts`мқҳ Phase D лёҢлЎңм»Ө publishк°Җ `digested` кІ°кіјм—җм„ңлҸ„ л°ңн–үлҗҳлҸ„лЎқ(мҳҲмӮ°мқҖ н‘ёмӢң мұ„л„җл§Ң кІҢмқҙнҠё, мқҙлҜё м—ҙлҰ° лқјмқҙлёҢ мҠӨнҠёлҰјмқҖ л¬ҙкҙҖ) мқҙлҸҷ. н…ҢмҠӨнҠё: stores 2к°ң мӢ к·ң(`digest-sent-store`) + proactivity(`digest-flush` 10 + pattern-firing broker-on-digest 1) + api(`digest-tick` 8) + cli(`commands-daemon` 3 + `commands-digest` 8) вҖ” м „л¶Җ fake-clock, к·ёлҰ°. м •м§Ғн•ң н•ңкі„: recap.tsмқҳ `safeRecapText`(injection-span мӨ‘нҷ”)к°Җ digest лқјмқём—җлҠ” м Ғмҡ©лҗҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ вҖ” нҒҗ н…ҚмҠӨнҠёлҠ” "мқҙлҜё мһҗкё° лЈЁн”„мқҳ кІҢмқҙнҠёлҘј нҶөкіјн•ң" кІғмқҙлқјлҠ” B1 л¶ҲліҖмӢқмқ„ к·ёлҢҖлЎң л”°лһҗкі , 5к°ң мҶҢмҠӨ лЈЁн”„ мһҗмІҙлҸ„ л°ңмҶЎ м „ мқҙ мӨ‘нҷ”лҘј м Ғмҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ” кё°мЎҙ м»ЁлІӨм…ҳкіј мқјкҙҖлҗЁ(лі„лҸ„ кІҖнҶ  лҢҖмғҒмңјлЎң лӮЁк№Җ). нҸүк°Җмһҗ PASS нӣ„ м»Өл°Ӣ лҢҖкё°.

- вң“ **assistant-rhythm S3 вҖ” мұ„л„җ лҰ¬л“¬ лқјмқҙлёҢ кІҖмҰқ л°°н„°лҰ¬ + л¬ём„ң** (worktree `assistant-rhythm`; S1 casual fast-pathВ·S2 delegation ackлҠ” мқҙлҜё м»Өл°ӢлҗЁ): `eval:channel-rhythm`(scripts/eval-channel-rhythm.mjs) вҖ” мӢӨ `createComposeAck`(apps/api)лҘј лЎңм»¬ gemma4:12bм—җ нғңмӣҢ KO+EN мң„мһ„мҡ”мІӯ 10кұҙ(ліөм°Ҫмқҙ non-nullВ·200мһҗ мқҙн•ҳВ·лӢЁмқјн–үВ·м–ём–ҙ мқјм№ҳВ·н”„лЎ¬н”„нҠё лҰ¬н„°лҹҙ echoВ·мқёмҡ©л§Ҳм»Ө з„Ў, м „л¶Җ кІ°м •лЎ  мұ„м җ)кіј casual 4кұҙ(`classifyCasualPrompt`к°Җ мғҒлҘҳм—җм„ң мһЎм•„ composer мһҗмІҙк°Җ м•Ҳ лҸҺмқ„ мҰқлӘ…)мқ„ кІҖмҰқ. pass^3 м•Ҳм •(MUSE_EVAL_REPEAT=3 л°ҳліө мӢӨн–ү лҢҖл¶Җл¶„ 14/14, нҸүк°Җмһҗ кҙҖмёЎ 1нҡҢ 12/14=86%лЎң 85% кІҢмқҙнҠё нҶөкіј вҖ” кІҢмқҙнҠё лӢЁмң„ м „ мӢӨн–ү PASS, мјҖмқҙмҠӨ лӢЁмң„ мҷ„м „ л¬ҙкІ°мқҖ м•„лӢҳ). `eval:agent` лІҲл“Ө нҺёмһ… + `pnpm eval:channel-rhythm` лӢЁлҸ… мҠӨнҒ¬лҰҪнҠё. FEATURES.md "м–‘л°©н–Ҙ мұ„л„җ лҢҖнҷ”" м Ҳм—җ лҢҖнҷ”-лҰ¬л“¬(ліөм°ҪвҶ’мЎ°мҡ©н•ң мҲҳн–үвҶ’мқёмҡ© мҷ„лЈҢ, `MUSE_CHANNEL_ACK=false`, мһ¬мӢңлҸ„-мӢң ліөм°Ҫ л°ҳліө к°ҖлҠҘ нҠңлӢқл©”лӘЁ) м„ңмҲ  м¶”к°Җ. нҸүк°Җмһҗ PASS нӣ„ м»Өл°Ӣ/лЁём§Җ лҢҖкё°.

- вҳ… A+ ROADMAP (2026-07-11, `docs/strategy/competitor-analysis-and-a-plus-roadmap.md`): 3-лқјмҡҙл“ң кІҪмҹҒмӮ¬(openclaw/hermes MIT) м ҒлҢҖ кІҖмҰқ нӣ„ B-м°Ёмӣҗ(agent-loopВ·securityВ·orchestrationВ·toolsВ·model-posture)мқ„ A+лЎң мҳ¬лҰ¬лҠ” 34-мҠ¬лқјмқҙмҠӨ нҒҗ + мӢӨн–ү мІҙнҒ¬лҰ¬мҠӨнҠё(В§10) + мӮҙм•„мһҲлҠ” кІҖмҰқ нҒҗ(В§11, м°©мҲҳ-м°ЁлӢЁ VQ 11 м „лҹү н•ҙмҶҢ). SHIPPED so far: вң“ **D1-S2** post-compaction лЈЁн”„к°Җл“ң(`PostCompactionLoopGuard`, agent-core, м»ҙнҢ©м…ҳ нӣ„ лҸҷмқј tool+args+result 3м—°мҶҚвҶ’abort; 15 testВ·mutation 5 REDВ·лҸ…лҰҪнҸүк°Җмһҗ PASS; b2822d12). вң“ **D2-S1a** seatbelt SBPL н”„лЎңнҢҢмқј мғқм„ұкё°(`build_seatbelt_profile`+`escape_sbpl_string`, crates/runner, мҲңмҲҳВ·лҜёл°°м„ В·мқём қм…ҳ мқҙмҠӨмјҖмқҙн”„ кІҖмҰқ; 26 test). NEXT: D2-S1b(л°°м„ +мӢӨн”„лЎңм„ёмҠӨ нғҲм¶ң н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, macOS attended).

- **D3-S2 лӢЁмқј-run heartbeat л°°м„  (agent-core мӢңмһ„ мҷ„лЈҢ, л Ҳм§ҖмҠӨнҠёлҰ¬ л°°м„ мқҖ лҜёмҷ„ вҖ” м•„лһҳ нӣ„мҶҚ н•ӯлӘ©)**: `ModelLoopRunner.heartbeat?: (runId: string) => void`(model-loop.ts) м¶”к°Җ вҖ” мӢ к·ң к°җм§Җкё° м•„лӢҳ, кё°мЎҙ `SubAgentRunRegistry.detectStalled`/`markStalledAsTimedOut` мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© лӘ©м Ғмқҳ мҲңмҲҳ мҪңл°ұ. л°©м¶ңм җ 3кіі: `streamModelTurn`мқҳ `text-delta`/`tool-call` мқҙлІӨнҠё мІҳлҰ¬л¶Җ + `runToolBatch`мқҳ GENUINE мӢӨн–ү(Phase 2, мӨ‘ліө/м°ЁлӢЁ/deadline м•„лӢҢ мӢӨм ң мӢӨн–ү) 1кұҙлӢ№ 1нҡҢ. throw-safe(`emitHeartbeat` try/catch, best-effort вҖ” мҪңл°ұмқҙ лҚҳм ёлҸ„ лЈЁн”„лҠ” м ҲлҢҖ м•Ҳ к№Ём§җ). `AgentRuntimeOptions.heartbeat`к°Җ `modelLoopRunner()`лЎң л°°м„ (agent-core лӮҙл¶Җ мҷ„кІ°, `@muse/multi-agent` import м—ҶмқҢ вҖ” мқҳмЎҙм„ұ л°©н–Ҙ л¶ҲліҖ). лҜёмЈјмһ… мӢң л°”мқҙнҠё-лҸҷмқј(4 emission test нҷ•мқё). н…ҢмҠӨнҠё: agent-core `model-loop-heartbeat.test.ts`(4 вҖ” text-delta+tool-call м№ҙмҡҙнҠё, нҲҙ-only м№ҙмҡҙнҠё м •л°Җ кІҖмҰқ, heartbeat м—ҶмқҢ=л¬ҙліҖнҷ”, throw л¬ҙн•ҙ) + multi-agent `subagent-run-registry-progress-heartbeat.test.ts`(2 вҖ” fake-clock: м§„н–ү мӨ‘ л°ҳліө heartbeatлҠ” мһҘмӢңк°„ streamлҸ„ мҳӨнғҗ м—ҶмқҢ / heartbeat мӨ‘лӢЁ мӢң timeout кІҪкіјн•ҳл©ҙ detectStalledк°Җ м •нҷ•нһҲ мһЎмқҢ). м–‘мӘҪ mutation-RED нҷ•мқё нӣ„ мӣҗліө(runToolBatch л°©м¶ң м ңкұ°вҶ’tool-count н…ҢмҠӨнҠё RED; multi-agent stall н…ҢмҠӨнҠём—җ "silence мӨ‘м—җлҸ„ heartbeat кі„мҶҚ" ліҖмқҙ мЈјмһ…вҶ’[]лЎң л’Өм§‘нһҳ, н…ҢмҠӨнҠёк°Җ vacuous м•„лӢҳмқ„ мҰқлӘ…). в—Ұ **DEFERRED (л Ҳм§ҖмҠӨнҠёлҰ¬ мӢӨл°°м„ )**: мҳӨлҠҳ л°ңкІ¬н•ң мӢӨм ң л°°м„  м§Җм җ вҖ” `AgentRuntime`мқҖ `packages/autoconfigure/src/runtime-assembly.ts`мқҳ `createAgentRuntime(...)` н•ң кіім—җм„ңл§Ң мғқм„ұлҗҳлҠ” лӢЁмқј кіөмң  мқёмҠӨн„ҙмҠӨмқҙкі , `apps/api/src/multi-agent-routes.ts`мқҳ `registerMultiAgentRoutes`лҠ” к·ё **к°ҷмқҖ мқёмҠӨн„ҙмҠӨ**лҘј `options.agentRuntime`мңјлЎң л°ӣмңјл©ҙм„ң мһҗкё° own `new SubAgentRunRegistry()`лҘј **лӮҳмӨ‘м—җ** л§Ңл“ лӢӨ(server.ts:229, runRegistry лҜём „лӢ¬) вҖ” мҰү л Ҳм§ҖмҠӨнҠёлҰ¬к°Җ AgentRuntime мғқм„ұ мӢңм җм—” м•„м§Ғ м—ҶмқҢ. orchestrator.ts нҷ•мқё кІ°кіј л¶ҖлӘЁ runмқҖ `registerParentRun(runId)`мңјлЎң **parentмқҳ runId к·ёлҢҖлЎң** л“ұлЎқлҗҳкі , мӣҢм»Ө мӢӨн–ү мӢң `input.runId`к°Җ childлЎң мһ¬кё°лЎқлҗҳм§Җ м•Ҡм•„(`withSelectedWorker`к°Җ мң м§Җ) workerмқҳ `context.runId`лҠ” мӢӨм ңлЎң parent runIdмҷҖ к°ҷлӢӨ вҖ” мҰү кіөмң  AgentRuntimeмқҙ heartbeat(parent runId)лҘј л°©м¶ңн•ҳл©ҙ к·ё registry entryк°Җ м •нҷ•нһҲ к°ұмӢ лҗ  мҲҳ мһҲлҠ” кө¬мЎ°(к°Җм§ң м•„лӢҳ, мӢӨм ңлЎң л§һл¬јлҰј). к·ёлҹ¬лӮҳ мқҙлҘј мӢӨл°°м„ н•ҳл Өл©ҙ (a) `@muse/autoconfigure`м—җ `@muse/multi-agent` мӢ к·ң мқҳмЎҙм„ұ м¶”к°Җ(нҢЁнӮӨм§Җ к·ёлһҳн”„ нҷ•мһҘ) лҳҗлҠ” (b) `AgentRuntime`м—җ мғқм„ұ-нӣ„ heartbeat м„ён„° м¶”к°Җ + `apps/api/server.ts`м—җм„ң registryлҘј лЁјм Җ л§Ңл“Өм–ҙ м–‘мӘҪ(л“ұлЎқ + AgentRuntime)м—җ лҸҷмқј мқёмҠӨн„ҙмҠӨлЎң мЈјмһ… вҖ” л‘ҳ лӢӨ apps/api/packages кІҪкі„лҘј л„ҳлҠ” лі„лҸ„ м„Өкі„ кІ°м •мқҙлқј мқҙлІҲ мҠ¬лқјмқҙмҠӨ лІ”мң„ л°–(м—”нғұкёҖ нҡҢн”ј, "к°Җм§ң л Ҳм§ҖмҠӨнҠёлҰ¬ кёҲм§Җ" мӣҗм№ҷ). NEXT: мң„ (a)/(b) мӨ‘ нғқ1лЎң мӢӨл°°м„  + `detectStalled`/`markStalledAsTimedOut` мҶҢл№„мһҗ(мЈјкё°м Ғ abort-on-stall нҸҙлҹ¬)к№Ңм§Җ мқҙм–ҙм•ј D3-S2к°Җ "лӢЁмқј run stallмқҙ мӢӨм ңлЎң к°җм§Җлҗҳм–ҙ мӨ‘лӢЁ"к№Ңм§Җ мҷ„кІ°.

byte-identical for extras-free callers (/api/ask, MCP recall вҖ” tests unmodified, deep-equal proof); second drive-by fix: refusal citation-strip was gated on note-style `citedSourcesIn` so an extra-category citation could survive on a refusal вҖ” now unconditional. вң“ RETROFIT SHIPPED (2026-07-10, same day): plain `muse ask` now routes through `streamGroundedRecall` вҖ” seam grew `composeSystemPrompt` / `normalizeAnswer` (pre-gate, buffered-only) / `extraChunks` / `result.scored` + `preRefusalStrippedCitations`, all byte-identical-when-absent; - вң“ GROUNDING EDGE fix (found by probing the real ask path вҖ” grounding-side dogfood): the citation-RECALL check (`reportCitationRecall`) falsely flagged an honest ABSTENTION ("I'm afraid I do not have a specific timeвҖҰ") as "matches your notes but carries no citation". Root cause: a broad evidence union (the note + 20 tasks + 4 reminders) inflated token overlap so the abstention looked 'citable', then was flagged as uncited вҖ” PUNISHING the exact behavior the edge wants (abstain over fabricate). Fix: `isAbstentionSentence` (EN+KO self-knowledge negation) excludes abstentions from the citable set. agent-core 2692 + citation-recall-abstention 13 (incl. a REGRESSION GUARD that a genuine uncited claim is still flagged) + mutation (drop the guard вҶ’ RED) + LIVE re-probe (same question, the false вҡ пёҸ warning is gone, abstention + `[from вҖҰ]` citation intact). The edge's fabrication=0 held throughout both probes (no fabricated time); this hardens its PRECISION (no false warning on honesty).

All live-verified. LESSON: mechanism-complete вү  usable вҖ” the CRUD/feedback gaps only showed by actually USING it. Minor follow-up left: `board clear` (rm covers it). Next direction options unchanged: cloud live round-trip (needs user key) В· return to the grounding/learning CORE edge (untouched this session вҖ” the actual moat).
- вң“ OPS BOARD zombie/liveness recovery (the last assessment gap vs hermes). `staleInProgressTasks`/`reclaimStaleTasks` (pure): a task stuck `in_progress` past a window (30 min default, `MUSE_BOARD_STALE_MS`) = a crashed run (the board is otherwise synchronous) вҶ’ moved to `blocked`, NOT auto-re-queued (a crash may have half-applied a side effect + the in-memory dedup is gone, so auto-rerun = double-execute вҖ” outbound-safety, same hazard as resume). `muse board reclaim` + auto-reclaim at the top of `board run` (a zombie would else block its dependents forever). multi-agent 327 + cli board 23 + mutation (reclaimвҶ’todo вҶ’ the no-auto-requeue test RED) + live (`board reclaim` unstuck a zombie вҶ’ blocked+reason). вң“ visual UI DONE вҖ” `GET /api/board` (board-routes.ts, read-only feed of the same persisted board the CLI drives, injectable listTasks) + a web Kanban `BoardView` (columns todoвҶ’done, container/synthesis badges, dep counts, blockedReason, horizontal-scroll bounded inside `.content`) wired into NAV (key "b") + i18n. api board-routes 2/2 + real-browser verify (Playwright: heading "ліҙл“ң", columns render, container/review/blocked cards shown, `.content` 968px bounded in a 1200px viewport вҖ” no blowout). OPS BOARD now feature-complete incl. the UI; only WRITE actions from the web (add/move/run) remain optional.

- вң“ OPS MULTI-AGENT вҖ” durable Kanban board, S1вҖ“S6 COMPLETE (2026-06-28, Jinan pivot to match openclaw/hermes). `@muse/multi-agent`: **S1** pure board core (`task-board.ts` вҖ” dependency-gated `nextReadyTask`, transitions, retry-with-reason) В· **S2** `board-store.ts` FileAgentTaskBoard (atomic persist, missing/corruptвҶ’[]) В· **S3** `dispatch-board.ts` `dispatchNextTask` (next-ready вҶ’ injected executor вҶ’ outcome folded back; thrownвҶ’blocked; retry replays prior reason) В· **S5** `tasksFromSubtasks` (decompositionвҶ’board tasks, dependsOn = fan-in gate) В· **S6** `resolveReview` + executor `needsReview` (outbound parks in REVIEW, approveвҶ’done/rejectвҶ’blocked). **S4** `muse board` CLI (add/list/move/retry/review/run; outbound titles drafted+parked, never sent вҖ” executor has NO transmission path at all). Verified: multi-agent 310 + cli board 12 + mutation + live (standalone `board run` completed a real agent task; store+dispatch+review live round-trip; retry-with-reason live) + independent evaluator PASS (outbound-safety deterministic). вң“ FOLLOW-UP #1: the `board run` executor now runs each task through the real `agentRuntime.run` (tools + grounding + the agent loop), NOT a single generate вҖ” proven live (a task used `muse.math.evaluate` + completed); a fail-closed `boardToolApprovalGate` allows READ tools but DENIES write/execute (an unattended run never auto-sends вҖ” outbound stays the review column's job), and a retry replays the prior failure into the prompt. cli board 15 + mutation + test:changed 1334. вң“ FOLLOW-UP #2 BOARD-AS-HANDOFF: a complex task EXPANDS into a sub-task DAG. `expandTaskIntoSubtasks` (pure) spawns the sub-tasks as a sequential chain (s_i deps s_{i-1}, matching decomposeRequest's ordered steps), rewires the parent to depend on them all + flags it `decomposed` вҶ’ it becomes a CONTAINER the dispatcher auto-completes (no executor run) once the sub-tasks finish. `muse board expand <id>` uses the deterministic `decomposeRequest` (no LLM). multi-agent 314 + cli board 15 + mutation (drop container auto-complete вҶ’ RED) + live (CLI expand вҶ’ chain вҶ’ DAG runs in order вҶ’ parent auto-completes). вң“ FOLLOW-UP #3: `muse board seed` turns your ACTIVE standing objectives into board tasks (`selectObjectiveSpecsToSeed` вҖ” active-only, deduped by title, idempotent; done/cancelled skipped). cli board 17 + live. вң— synthesis-context DROPPED as over-engineering: decomposeRequest yields SEQUENTIAL chains where the LAST sub-task already IS the synthesis ("research вҶ’ summarize"), so a separate container-synthesis adds nothing until we have PARALLEL/independent sub-tasks (which we don't generate) вҖ” revisit only if parallel decomposition lands. OPS BOARD = feature-complete for the personal scope. вң“ FOLLOW-UP #3 (partial вҖ” parallel decomposition): `expandTaskIntoSubtasks` gained a `mode` ("sequential" default = chain; "parallel" = INDEPENDENT sub-tasks, all immediately runnable), exposed as `muse board expand <id> --parallel`. multi-agent 23 + cli 17 + mutation (parallel-also-chains вҶ’ RED) + live (`--parallel` split an "вҖҰand thenвҖҰ" task into 2 deps=[] sub-tasks). вң— NOT built (honest, anti-over-engineering): the LLM AUTO parallel-DECOMPOSER + combined SYNTHESIS вҖ” the deterministic decomposeRequest yields ZERO parallel splits (proven: 7 probes вҶ’ 0 parallel) and mostly n=1, so a synthesis run has no parallel source to combine; building it now repeats the synthesis-context trap. вң“ NOW DONE вҖ” LLM parallel decomposer + synthesis: `parallel-decompose.ts` (`planParallelSubtasks`/`parseParallelPlan` вҖ” the model splits a goal into INDEPENDENT sub-tasks, "NONE"вҶ’[] abstain); a parallel expansion flags the container `synthesize`; the dispatcher runs a synthesize container's executor over its sub-tasks' stored outputs (`TaskRun.output`/`AgentTask.result`/`latestOutput` + `ctx.dependencyOutputs`) to COMBINE them, vs auto-complete for sequential. `board expand` default = LLM parallel (fallback sequential); `boardTaskPrompt` builds the synthesis prompt; executor still gated read-only. LIVE: "compare Python vs Rust" вҶ’ 5 independent sub-tasks вҶ’ fan-out вҶ’ synthesis combined all 5. multi-agent 323 + cli board 20 + mutation (synthesizeвҶ’auto-complete RED) + e2e. вң“ CLOUD BYO-KEY (#1/#2): `muse setup cloud` wizard (planCloudSetup, 6 tests) + createModelProvider cloud-routing gate test (4) вҖ” provider-neutral path verified (local-only fail-close intact).

- вң“ RESUME SAFETY (other half): per-tool checkpoint inside a MULTI-tool batch. The checkpoint was written only AFTER runToolBatch (post-batch), so a crash BETWEEN two tools in one model response lost the already-run ones вҶ’ they weren't in the replayed transcript вҶ’ the dedup-seeding couldn't guard them вҶ’ re-execution. Now a >1-tool batch checkpoints after EACH tool's result message (`[...messages, ...toolMessages]`, distinct step). A 1-tool batch (the norm) is unchanged (post-batch covers it). execute-model-loop 18/18 (+ multi-tool checkpoints-step-1) + mutation (drop it вҶ’ RED), agent-core 2679. Together with the dedup-seeding (c46b98aee), resume is now fully double-execution-safe even for parallel tool calls.

- вң“ RESUME SAFETY: a resumed run no longer RE-EXECUTES a completed side-effecting tool (re-send/re-book) вҖ” the tool-call deduplicator was in-memory + reset on resume, so a re-issued call after a crash had no guard. `seedDeduplicatorFromHistory` re-records each COMPLETED tool call from the replayed messages (mutating = risk write|execute, matching the live path) in BOTH loops; a crash-point in-flight call (no result) is left runnable, a non-resume run is a no-op. 4/4 unit (re-exec deduped / different-args runs / non-resume no-op / crash-point runnable) + mutation (no-op seed вҶ’ RED), agent-core 2678, independent evaluator PASS. Closes the agent-loop-robustness audit's resume-idempotency gap (ties to outbound-safety: no autonomous double-send).

- вң“ encryption-at-rest for BELIEF-PROVENANCE (where each remembered fact about you came from) вҖ” @muse/memory can't use the @muse/stores seam (cycle: storesвҶ’memory for the envelope fns), so it mirrors the proven in-package memory-user-store-file pattern (read isEncryptedMemoryEnvelopeвҶ’decrypt fail-CLOSED; write format-preserving via isBeliefProvenanceEncrypted; env threaded through FileBeliefProvenanceStore). `muse memory encrypt`/`decrypt` now cover facts + provenance in lock-step (best-effort). Round-trip 3/3 (envelope, no plaintext value, wrong-key throws, format preserved), memory 622, independent evaluator PASS (no fs bypass, fail-closed verified). в—Ұ LAST encryption queue item: the calendar store (events/locations вҖ” sensitive); notes-index intentionally plaintext.

- вң“ encryption-at-rest for REFLECTIONS ("what Muse noticed about you") вҖ” reflections-store routed through the proven readMaybeEncrypted/writeMaybeEncrypted seam (format-preserving, fail-CLOSED on wrong key) + `muse reflections encrypt|decrypt|encryption-status` commands + privacy-dashboard def. Round-trip 3/3 (aes-256-gcm envelope, ciphertext lacks the insight, wrong-key throws, format preserved), independent evaluator PASS (no fs bypass across 7 call sites). The proven per-store TEMPLATE for the remaining plaintext stores. в—Ұ NEXT (same template): belief-provenance.json (@muse/memory вҖ” facts-about-user) + calendar store; notes-index intentionally left plaintext (large + embeddings, low marginal value).

- вң“ grounding-corpus write integrity вҖ” notes-index `saveIndex` + note-provenance `recordIngestedNote` routed from RAW non-atomic writeFile вҶ’ the proven `atomicWriteFile` (tmp+fsync+rename, 0o600). A crash mid-write was silently corrupting the recall corpus / `[from вҖҰ]` citation ledger (= the FUNCTIONAL EDGE's backbone). note-provenance 6/6 (no .tmp orphan + valid-JSON under 12 concurrent writes), atomic-file-store 10/10 owns the atomicity teeth, independent evaluator PASS. в—Ұ NEXT internal-hardening queue (2026-06-28 audit, code-grounded): (a) **enforceAnswerCitations leaves the fabricated CLAIM sentence when it strips an unresolved citation marker** вҖ” a fabrication-leak in the citation gate, drop the clause not just the marker (knowledge-recall.ts ~453); (b) encryption coverage вҖ” calendar.json/notes-index/reflections/belief-provenance still PLAINTEXT (extend encrypted-file.ts pattern); (c) вҸі corroboration quorum default-on (MUSE_QUORUM_HEDGE OFF by default вҖ” posture call); (d) novel-injection deterministic backstop (8B ignores the prompt header вҖ” hard frontier).

- вң“ DX: `pnpm test:changed` (scripts/test-changed.mjs) вҖ” run ONLY the vitest-`related` tests of git-changed files per affected package, not a whole package suite. Closes the "5-min wait per edit" pain (Muse has ~12.8k cases/1194 files вҖ” healthy vs openclaw's 6568 test files / hermes' 2006, verified 2026-06-26; the waste was running ALL per edit). Verified: a runtime-helpers.ts edit вҶ’ 1300 tests vs full agent-core 2668; leaf files run a handful. Wired into CLAUDE.md dev-cycle + testing.md narrowest-test rule (`pnpm check` stays the pre-merge gate). 2026 best practice for a vitest stack = native module-graph `related` + git diff, no Nx/Turbo needed.

- в—Ұ internal-hardening (2026-06-28, audit-driven, 4 code-grounded auditors): вң… R1 streaming idle-timeout (hung Ollama stream no longer hangs the agent вҖ” likely the smoke:live stall; agent-core withStreamIdleTimeout) В· вң… R3 programming-error retries fail-fast (TypeError/ReferenceError/RangeError; SyntaxError EXCLUDED = transient provider-garbage) В· вҸӯпёҸ R2 claim-screen fail-open left as a documented soft-probe trade-off (not a hard-gate inversion; fabrication=0 gate is separate+fail-close; product call) В· вң“ **M1 god-file decomp DONE**: commands-ask.ts **2827вҶ’2280 (-547)** via 8 behavior-preserving slices вҖ” 4 helper modules (ask-corpus-helpers, ask-user-data-presence, ask-image-attachments, ask-prompt-constants) + 4 orchestration (ask-session-grounding [episodes/feed/reflection], ask-note-retrieval [the RAG core: embed/MMR/graph/2nd-hop], ask-activity-grounding [shell/git/action], ask-personal-store-grounding [tasks/calendar/reminders/contacts]). ### Langchain/langgraph-parity assessment (2026-06-28) вҖ” shipped 5, the rest are honest limits

A capability audit vs langchain/langgraph: Muse provides every core agent primitive
(chains/ReAct, tools, memory, lead-worker orchestration, HITL approval, durable
run-state, streaming) hand-rolled, AND adds differentiators they lack (the deterministic
grounding+citation gate, local-first fail-close egress, correction-decay learning,
baked-in evals, security-as-code). SHIPPED this session (each: tests+mutation+independent
evaluator+lint, commits below):

- вң“ **B4** eval:recall-quality honestly relabelled (it measures the cosine gate, not the
  lexical production memory path) + production `selectMemoryFacts` regression-locked.
- вң“ **B2** the proactive north-star LIVE battery now drives the PRODUCTION investigator
  (`createIndexedProactiveInvestigator`), not a generic test-helper (4/4 live).
- вң“ **B6** faithfulness pre-push tripwire 177sвҶ’96s (~46%) via a fabrication-SAFE subset
  (all drift+refuse kept вҶ’ faithfulness metric identical; only answerable sampled).
- вң“ **B1** chat misgroundings now labelled in the run-log (`chatTraceOutcome`) вҶ’ they
  become error-analysis FUEL instead of vanishing as grounded:null (ask had it, chat didn't).
- вң“ **A1** default-on cross-source corroboration signal ("вң“ corroborated by N sources")
  on the ask+chat wedge вҖ” the realistic local-first hedge against GROUNDEDвү TRUE.

NOT open work (inherent limits / deferred вҖ” do NOT re-scout as buildable):
- вӣ” **B3** multi-agent on a single GPU is a *phantom* (no true parallelism) вҖ” a hardware
  limit; the value is context-isolation+decomposition, already built. Not code-fixable.
- вӣ” **B5** local-12B one-shot tool-calling has load-amplified flakiness (eval:tools ~99%,
  KO followup.cancel / time_diff) вҖ” a model-capacity limit the deterministic harness
  mitigates but can't erase. Not code-fixable on a fixed model.
- вҸі **A2** reranker (Qwen3-Reranker-0.6B candidate, KO-MTEB-strong) вҖ” a real stretch but
  needs a model pull + an A/B eval proving the delta; human-gated (model choice).
- вҸі **A3** generic graph DSL + automatic full-state durability/time-travel (langgraph-style)
  вҖ” low priority for a single-user local agent (no arbitrary multi-agent topologies).
- вҸі **A4** async-announce non-polling sub-agent completion вҖ” deferred, low value on one GPU.

The one remaining FRONTIER (open, hard, high-value): full **source VERACITY** (GROUNDEDвү TRUE)
вҖ” impossible to fully solve under local-first (no external oracle); A1 corroboration is the
realistic partial hedge. Deeper veracity needs a human/product call, not an autonomous slice.

- вң“ work-status dashboard (`pnpm status` вҶ’ docs/status.html) вҖ” glanceable HTML from the MD records (recent commits color-coded В· backlog вҳ…/в—Ұ/вҸі/вң“ counts+lists В· self-eval gates) so a human sees "what got done / what's next / is it healthy" without reading code/git/3k-line backlog. `--watch [s]` regenerates on an interval + injects a meta-refresh so an open tab auto-updates (one-shot omits it). Pure parsers + watch helpers unit-tested 11/11, mutation-verified, HTML-injection escaped, gitignored artifact.
- вң“ risk-review (dashboard session) fixes: (a) **guard-writeback** now recognizes `scripts/*.test.mjs` as a compounding artifact (was `*.test.ts(x)` only вҶ’ script-only feats wrongly blocked); decision logic extracted to `stagesCompoundingArtifact()` + 7 node:test. (b) **precheck:grounding** faithfulness-rate was SKIP-on-every-push (real cost вүҲ177s > 150s cap вҶ’ a fabrication-critical gate silently never ran); raised per-battery timeout 150sвҶ’240s and made the pre-push a pass^1 tripwire (the authoritative pass^k stays in `eval:self-improving`). ## вҳ… 2026-07-07 BROWSING theme вҖ” "learns you" лҚ°мқҙн„° кё°к·ј н•ҙмҶҢ (м§„м•Ҳ-directed; ~/.museк°Җ л…ёнҠё 0к°ңВ·л©”лӘЁлҰ¬ 736BлЎң мӮ¬мӢӨмғҒ л№Ҳ кІғмқҙ л°ңкІ¬ кі„кё°)

- вң“ (231dbf30) Stage 1: Chrome History SQLite мқём ңмҠӨмІң вҖ” node:sqlite(мқҳмЎҙм„ұ 0), мһ кёҙ нҢҢмқј мһ„мӢңліөмӮ¬ нӣ„ мқҪкё°, BigInt visit_time(>2^53), http/https н•„н„°, 0o600 мҠӨнҶ м–ҙ, `muse browsing sync|search|recent` + `browsing_search` нҲҙ(eval:tools 4/4 STABLE 3/3). лӘ…мӢңм Ғ syncк°Җ кі§ лҸҷмқҳ вҖ” лҚ°лӘ¬мқҖ Chrome нҢҢмқј м ҲлҢҖ м•Ҳ мқҪмқҢ. мӢӨ н”„лЎңн•„ 1985л°©л¬ё лқјмқҙлёҢ кІҖмҰқ, лҸ…лҰҪнҸүк°Җ 7/7 PASS. ToS/м •мұ… кІҖнҶ  мҷ„лЈҢ(л¬ём ңм—ҶмқҢ вҖ” Firefox import м„ лЎҖ, нҸүл¬ё нҢҢмқј, м•”нҳёнҷ” мҡ°нҡҢ м—ҶмқҢ).
- вң“ (41b03ac8) Stage 2: ask grounded-recall нҶөн•© вҖ” 12лІҲм§ё мқёмҡ© л§Ҳм»Ө `[browsing: <hostname>]`(exact-match, false-KEEP л¶Ҳк°Җ), CJK-aware л үмӢңм»¬ м„ нғқ, feedsмҷҖ л°”мқҙнҠё лҸҷмқј мқём қм…ҳ мқҙмҠӨмјҖмқҙн”„, untrustedBrowsingMatch(trusted:false) ask+verdict м–‘кІҪлЎң, рҹҢҗ мҳҒмҲҳмҰқ. gemma4 лқјмқҙлёҢ лқјмҡҙл“ңнҠёлҰҪ л№ҢлҚ”+нҸүк°Җмһҗ мқҙмӨ‘ кІҖмҰқ. groundedSurfaces н”ҢлЎңм–ҙ мң м§Җ(30).
- вң“ (2d4d490d) Stage 3a: лҚ°лӘ¬ opt-in мһҗлҸҷ sync вҖ” MUSE_BROWSING_AUTO_SYNC(кё°ліё off), 60л¶„ мҠӨлЎңнӢҖ, sync мҪ”м–ҙ @muse/recallлЎң м¶”м¶ң(м»Өл§Ёл“ң/лҚ°лӘ¬ кіөмң ). consent pin(кё°ліёк°’м—җм„ң Chrome м ‘к·ј 0нҡҢ, мҠӨнҢҢмқҙ seam=н”„лЎңлҚ•м…ҳ кІҪлЎң) л®Өн…Ңмқҙм…ҳ кІҖмҰқ. лҸ…лҰҪнҸүк°Җ 7/7 PASS.
- вң“ (39fd8506) Stage 3b: cross-lingual мһ„лІ л”© recall вҖ” sync мӢң нғҖмқҙнӢҖ мһ„лІ л”©(v2-moe, search_query:/search_document: н”„лҰ¬н”ҪмҠӨ н•„мҲҳ), н•ҳмқҙлёҢлҰ¬л“ң м„ нғқ(л үмӢңм»¬вҲӘмҪ”мӮ¬мқёвүҘ0.18), KOм§ҲмқҳвҶ’ENнғҖмқҙнӢҖ лқјмқҙлёҢ STABLE 3/3 + negative A/B мҰқлӘ…. merge-clobber лҰ¬мҠӨнҒ¬ нҸүк°Җмһҗ мЎ°мӮ¬лЎң л°ҳмҰқ(strict cursor + лі‘н•©нӣ„ мһ¬мһ„лІ л”©). fail-soft м „л°©мң„.
- вң“ (b28511d6) Stage 4: feeds cross-lingual вҖ” мқём ңмҠӨнҠё мӢң нғҖмқҙнӢҖ мһ„лІ л”© + recency лІ мқҙмҠӨ мң„ rescue м•”(л үмӢңм»¬вҲӘмҪ”мӮ¬мқёвүҘ0.18, no-vec вҮ’ л°”мқҙнҠё лҸҷмқј нҡҢк·Җн•Җ), мҝјлҰ¬ мһ„лІ л”© askлӢ№ 1нҡҢ feeds/browsing кіөмң . RSS нҠ№мң  merge-clobber(л§Ө refresh лҸҷмқј id мһ¬мҲҳмӢ  вҶ’ мһ„лІ л”© м „л©ё мң„н—ҳ)лҘј title-лҸҷмқј мәҗлҰ¬нҸ¬мӣҢл“ңлЎң н•ҙмҶҢ(5Г—-refresh м•Ҳм •м„ұ н•Җ, л®Өн…Ңмқҙм…ҳ RED нҷ•мқё). KOм§ҲмқҳвҶ’мңҲлҸ„мҡ° л°– EN н—Өл“ңлқјмқё `[feed:]` мқёмҡ© лқјмқҙлёҢ STABLE 2/2 + negative A/B. лҸ…лҰҪнҸүк°Җ 8/8 PASS.
- вң“ (644fc899) Stage 5: verify-browsing-recall(4мјҖмқҙмҠӨ) + verify-feed-crosslingual(3мјҖмқҙмҠӨ, negative A/B мҳҒкө¬нҷ”) лқјмқҙлёҢ л°°н„°лҰ¬ вҖ” мӢӨм ң нҢҢмқҙн”„лқјмқё(м§„м§ң builder/normalizer/кІҢмқҙнҠё) кө¬лҸҷ, pass^4(л№ҢлҚ” 3/3 + нҸүк°Җмһҗ 1нҡҢ), groundedSurfaces лһҳм№« 30вҶ’32. лҸ…лҰҪнҸүк°Җ 7/7 PASS.
- в—Ұ мһ”м—¬ нӣ„ліҙ: мҠӨнҶ м–ҙ sidecar л¶„лҰ¬ кІҖнҶ (browsing ~21MB@2000 вҖ” м»Өм§Җл©ҙ); `--json` grounded лё”лЎқ нҢЁлҰ¬нӢ°(feeds/browsing л‘ҳ лӢӨ л№ м§җ) вҸім§„м•Ҳ кІ°м •; лёҢлқјмҡ°м§•/н”јл“ң н…Ңл§Ҳ вҶ’ proactive/recap м—°кІ°("мҡ”мҰҳ X л§Һмқҙ ліҙмӢңл„Өмҡ”").
- вң“ (50b0a319) в‘  vision н•ңкёҖ м»ӨлІ„лҰ¬м§Җ вҖ” мёЎм •мқҙ к°Җм„Өмқ„ л’Өм§‘мқҢ: gemma4 6/6+5/5(н•ңкёҖ м „мҠ№) vs qwen3-vl 4/6(мқҙлІӨнҠё мҠӨнӮӨл§Ҳ л№Ҳм¶ңл Ҙ, н•ңмҳҒ кіөнҶө 3/3) вҶ’ **кё°ліёк°’ мң м§Җ**, н•ңкёҖ н”ҪмҠӨмІҳ 2мў… мҳҒкө¬ кІҢмқҙнҠёнҷ” + MUSE_VISION_MODEL л…ёлёҢ(fail-soft) л°°мҶЎ. мғқнғңкі„ лҰ¬м„ңм№ҳлҸ„ мҲҳл ҙ(openclaw лЎңм»¬ кё°ліёк°’=gemma4, /v1 кІҪлЎң нҲҙмҪңл§Ғ м—ҙнҷ” кІҪкі  вҶ’ Ollama л„ӨмқҙнӢ°лёҢ мң м§Җ нҷ•м •). qwen3.5лҠ” Ollama mmproj/нҲҙмҪң н…ңн”ҢлҰҝ м„ұмҲҷ мӢң мһ¬нҸүк°Җ.
- вҳ… NEXT-THEME нӣ„ліҙ (2026-07-07 к°ӯмҠӨм№ҙмҡ°нҠё, мғҒм„ёлҠ” м„ём…ҳ ліҙкі ): в‘Ў iMessage chat.db мқём ңмҠӨмІң(вҸім§„м•Ҳ мқҙм—° вҖ” мһ¬м ңм•Ҳ кёҲм§Җ, м§„м•Ҳмқҙ лӢӨмӢң м—ҙ л•Ңк№Ңм§Җ); вң“в‘ў н•ңкөӯм–ҙ voice кё°ліёк°’ вҖ” DONE(4c06b3cf, v0.2.15); вң“ мҳЁліҙл”© лҚ°мқҙн„° мң„м Җл“ң вҖ” DONE(abc4da38, v0.2.17): muse setup data, лҸҷмқҳ кё°ліё NO+л®Өн…Ңмқҙм…ҳ н•Җ, MUSE_* н•ҳмқҙл“ңл Ҳмқҙм…ҳ л¶Җмһ¬ нҷ•мқё нӣ„ export лё”лЎқ л°©мӢқ(м •м§Ғ), мҳЁліҙл”© нһҢнҠё м—°кІ°; в‘Ј macOS м—°лқҪмІҳ мһ„нҸ¬нҠё + мҳЁліҙл”© мһ„нҸ¬нҠё мң„м Җл“ң(S); вң“в‘Ө мәҳлҰ°лҚ” м“°кё° вҖ” **CONVERGED/мқҙлҜё м „лҹү л°°мҶЎ** (2026-07-07 кІҖмҰқ: м „ provider createEvent + CLI add/edit/delete + muse.calendar.add кІҢмқҙнҠё + eval 13/13 pass^3 н•ңкөӯм–ҙ нҸ¬н•Ё + deny-л¬ҙнҡЁкіј кі„м•Ҫн…ҢмҠӨнҠё вҖ” к°ӯмҠӨм№ҙмҡ°нҠёк°Җ лӮЎмқҖ "read-only" л¬ёмһҗм—ҙм—җ мҶҚмқҢ, cee1459dлЎң л¬ёмһҗм—ҙл§Ң мҲҳм •. мһ¬м ңм•Ҳ кёҲм§Җ); в‘Ҙ н”„лқјмқҙлІ„мӢң-кі„мёө нҒҙлқјмҡ°л“ң лқјмҡ°нҢ…(к°ңмқё м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё мЈјмһ… askлҠ” л¬ҙмЎ°кұҙ лЎңм»¬, л¬ҙмЈјмһ… мқјл°ҳ м§Ҳл¬ёл§Ң мҳөнҠёмқё нҒҙлқјмҡ°л“ң вҖ” ask-tier-models мқён”„лқј мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©).

## вҳ… macOS м»ӨлІ„лҰ¬м§Җ л§ө (2026-07-07 мҠӨм№ҙмҡ°нҠё, м§„м•Ҳ directive "л§Ҙм—җм„ң мҷ л§Ңн•ң кұҙ лӢӨ лҗҳкІҢ вҖ” м •мұ… м•Ҳм—җм„ң")

мҠӨмҪ”м–ҙліҙл“ң: л№„м„ң-кҙҖл Ё 26к°ң лҠҘл Ҙ мӨ‘ **ліҙмң  16 / л№Ңл“ңк°ҖлҠҘ 7 / м •мұ…м ңмҷёВ·мқҙм—° 3**. м •мұ… н•„н„° мӢӨмҪ”л“ң нҷ•мқё: osascript Apple-Events мһҗлҸҷнҷ” н—Ҳмҡ©(нҚјлІ мқҙмӢңлёҢ мӮ¬мҡ© мӨ‘), Tier-3 м ңмҷё = System Events нӮӨмһ…л Ҙ/нҒҙлҰӯ нҚјнҺҳнӢ°м–ҙл§Ғл§Ң(мқҪкё°лҠ” н—Ҳмҡ©), м“°кё°лҠ” MUSE_MACOS_ACTUATORS кІҢмқҙнҠё.

л№Ңл“ңк°ҖлҠҘ мҲңмң„(л№„м„ң к°Җм№ҳмҲң): вң“в‘  Apple Reminders вҖ” м§„м•Ҳ кІ°м • "Muse мҠӨнҶ м–ҙ+Apple лҜёлҹ¬(лӢЁл°©н–Ҙ)"лЎң н•ҙмҶҢ(068d2c70, v0.2.13): MUSE_APPLE_REMINDERS_MIRROR opt-in, лӘЁлҚё-facing нҲҙ мӢ м„Ө м—ҶмқҢ(нҳјлҸҷмҢҚ 0), мқём қм…ҳ 5-нҺҳмқҙлЎңл“ң л®Өн…Ңмқҙм…ҳ кІҖмҰқ, 3к°ң мғқм„ұ м§Җм җ нӣ…(мқҙмӨ‘л°ңмӮ¬ м—ҶмқҢ к°җмӮ¬), fail-soft. Notes лҜёлҹ¬лҸ„ к°ҷмқҖ нҢЁн„ҙ м Ғмҡ© мҳҲм • вң“в‘Ў Apple Notes лҜёлҹ¬ вҖ” DONE(f80090c1, v0.2.14): мқҳлҸ„м Ғ мғқм„ұл§Ң лҜёлҹ¬(ingest/мқјмқјмқёл°•мҠӨ/append/overwrite м ңмҷё вҖ” Notes.app мҠӨнҢё л°©м§Җ), 2мёө мқҙмҠӨмјҖмқҙн”„(HTML+AppleScript) к°Ғк°Ғ л®Өн…Ңмқҙм…ҳ кІҖмҰқ, recall мҪ”нҚјмҠӨ л°”мқҙнҠё л¶ҲліҖ мҰқлӘ…, кё°мЎҙ AppleNotesProviderмҷҖ мқҙмӨ‘м“°кё° м—ҶмқҢ нҸүк°Җмһҗ м¶”м Ғ. вҡ нӣ„мҶҚ: мӢӨкё°кё°м—җм„ң `<br>` л ҢлҚ” нҷ•мқё 1нҡҢ н•„мҡ”(Automation к¶Ңн•ң н•„мҡ”лқј мһҗлҸҷнҷ” л¶Ҳк°Җ) вң“в‘ў Focus/DND вҖ” DONE(0e259570, v0.2.15): mac_system_set enum нҷ•мһҘ(мӢ к·ң нҲҙ м—ҶмқҢ), Shortcuts нӮӨмҠӨнҶӨ, KO лЎңмјҖмқј мӢӨмәЎмІҳ кё°л°ҳ лҜёмЎҙмһ¬ к°җм§Җ+м…Ӣм—… м•ҲлӮҙ, eval 48/48 pass^3(ліјлҘЁ confusable нҸ¬н•Ё), doctor мІҙнҒ¬. н•ңкөӯм–ҙ voice кё°ліёк°’лҸ„ лҸҷмӢң л°°мҶЎ(4c06b3cf вҖ” лӢӨкөӯм–ҙ whisper кё°ліё+л Ҳкұ°мӢң нҸҙл°ұ, KSS лқјмқҙм„ мҠӨ лӘ…л¬ёнҷ”, doctor к°Җмқҙл“ң) вң“в‘Ј Apple м—°лқҪмІҳ мһ„нҸ¬нҠё вҖ” DONE(0477d981, v0.2.16): C0 кө¬л¶„мһҗ нҺҳмқҙлЎңл“ң(мЈјмһ…л©ҙ 0), split-before-strip, к°ҖмӮ°м Ғ лі‘н•©(мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ н•„л“ң л¶ҲліҖ, л©ұл“ұ), м—°лҸ„м—ҶлҠ” мғқмқјвҶ’мӢӨ resolveUpcomingBirthdays нҶөн•©н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, TCC fail-soft лқјмқҙлёҢ мҰқлӘ…. мһ”м—¬: Apple м—°лқҪмІҳ 'м¶”к°Җ'(м“°кё°)лҠ” лі„лҸ„ лҜём°©мҲҳ в‘Ө Photos кІҖмғү/лӮҙліҙлӮҙкё°(M) в‘Ҙ м•ұ мў…лЈҢ(S) в‘Ұ лӢӨнҒ¬лӘЁл“ң(S, мҠӨнҒ¬лҰҪнҢ… н”„лЎңнҚјнӢ°лқј Tier-3 м•„лӢҳ) в‘§ л°қкё°/лё”лЈЁнҲ¬мҠӨ(S, Shortcuts).

м •мұ…м ңмҷё лӘ…л¬ёнҷ”(мһ¬кІҖнҶ  л°©м§Җ): AirDrop м „мҶЎ(кіөмӢқ кІҪлЎң м—ҶмқҢвҶ’Tier-3 н•„мҡ”вҶ’м ңмҷё) В· мһ„мқҳ м•ұ UI нҚјнҺҳнӢ°м–ҙл§Ғ(Tier-3) В· мһҗмңЁ л°ңмҶЎ(draft-firstл§Ң) В· banking(мҳҒкө¬) В· brew мһ„мқҳ м„Өм№ҳ(runner кІҪмң  н•„мҲҳ). мқҙм—°: iMessage мқҪкё°(м§„м•Ҳ кІ°м •, FDA н•„мҡ”).

## вҳ… 2026-07-03 found-during-DS-7: withFileLock мһ¬мӢңлҸ„ кІҪн•©мқҙ н’Җ мҠӨмң„нҠё лі‘л ¬ л¶Җн•ҳм—җм„ң flaky (pre-existing, DS-3мҷҖ л¬ҙкҙҖ)

- в—Ұ packages/stores 54к°ң н…ҢмҠӨнҠё нҢҢмқјмқҙ vitest лі‘л · мӣҢм»ӨлЎң лҸҷмӢң мӢӨн–үлҗ  л•Ң consent/objectives/veto/proposed-action-concurrencyмқҳ 50-лі‘л ¬-writer н…ҢмҠӨнҠёк°Җ к°„н—җм ҒмңјлЎң `EEXIST .lock` + мқҙм–ҙм§ҖлҠ” `ENOTEMPTY rmdir`лЎң мӢӨнҢЁ (кІ©лҰ¬ мӢӨн–ү мӢң 16/16 к·ёлҰ° вҖ” лЎңл“ң мң л°ң, лЎңм§Ғ лІ„к·ё м•„лӢҳ). encrypted-file.jsмқҳ лқҪ мһ¬мӢңлҸ„ backoff/нҡҹмҲҳк°Җ мӢңмҠӨн…ң л¶Җн•ҳ н•ҳ 50-writer кІҪн•©мқ„ лӘ» лІ„нҢҖ. FIX нӣ„ліҙ: мһ¬мӢңлҸ„ нҡҹмҲҳ/backoff мғҒн•ң мғҒн–Ҙ лҳҗлҠ” м§ҖмҲҳ л°ұмҳӨн”„ jitter м¶”к°Җ, mkdirмңјлЎң мһ”м—¬ лқҪ л””л үнҶ лҰ¬ м •лҰ¬ лЎңм§Ғ м җкІҖ.

## вҳ… 2026-07-03 delta-scout ROUND 2 (7/2 мқҙнӣ„ мӢ к·ң 251+104 м»Өл°Ӣ, 3лҸ…лҰҪ мҠӨм№ҙмҡ°нҠё) вҖ” Tier 1 5кұҙ мҰүмӢңм°©мҲҳ, лӮҙл¶Җн’Ҳм§Ҳ л ҢмҰҲк°Җ "мқҙ л°©н–Ҙ мҶҢм§„" лӘ…мӢңм Ғ мӢ нҳё

Tier 1 (мһҗмІҙ мҪ”л“ң мӢӨлІ„к·ё, кі мӢ лў°, к·јкұ° нҷ•ліҙ):
- вң“ (DS-16, c7ef8ba4) MCP мЈҪмқҖ м„ём…ҳ self-heal вҖ” onclose/onerror л°°м„  + ensureLiveConnectionмқҙ лӢӨмқҢ нҳём¶ңм—җм„ң нҲ¬лӘ… мһ¬м—°кІ°, closure-stalenessлҸ„ resolveConnection мҪңл°ұмңјлЎң н•ҙкІ°, mid-refresh race 2кіі м°ЁлӢЁ. мӢӨм ң stdio мһҗмӢқ мў…лЈҢлЎң e2e кІҖмҰқ. 8 tests.
- вң“ (DS-17, ba111203) 8к°ң м§Җм җ м „л¶Җ мӢӨлІ„к·ё нҷ•мқё нӣ„ Buffer.concat-then-decode-onceлЎң нҶөмқј вҖ” 2кіімқҖ л°”мқҙнҠёмәЎвҶ’л¬ёмһҗмәЎ м „нҷҳмқҳ мқҳлҸ„м Ғ лҸҷмһ‘ліҖнҷ” лӘ…мӢң. 9 tests, 4к°ң нҢЁнӮӨм§Җ м „л¶Җ к·ёлҰ°.
- вң“ (DS-18, ad624b7a) @muse/resilienceмқҳ кё°мЎҙ retry() мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©(мӢ к·ң мқҳмЎҙм„ұ з„Ў), 250ms/500ms л°ұмҳӨн”„ 3нҡҢ мӢңлҸ„ нӣ„м—җл§Ң мҝЁлӢӨмҡҙ. л®Өн…Ңмқҙм…ҳ RED 6/10.
- вң“ (DS-19, 6664cce9) referenceMaxOutputTokens м¶”к°Җ вҖ” opt-in, лҜём„Өм •мӢң кё°мЎҙкіј byte-identical. 3 tests.
- вң“ (DS-20, fdea1953) кіөмң  н—¬нҚј backupVersionMismatchedStore вҖ” 3к°ң мҠӨнҶ м–ҙ м „л¶Җ rename-then-discardлЎң м „нҷҳ, fail-soft. 12 tests.

Tier 2 (мҷ„лЈҢ):

**лӮҙл¶Җн’Ҳм§Ҳ л ҢмҰҲ лӘ…мӢң к¶Ңкі **: "мқҙ л°©н–Ҙ(openclaw/hermes лӮҙл¶Җм—”м§ҖлӢҲм–ҙл§Ғ л№„көҗ) мҠӨм№ҙмҡ°нҠёлҠ” мқҙм ң мҶҢм§„ вҖ” лӮЁмқҖ кІҪмҹҒмӮ¬ нҲ¬мһҗ(Docker л©ҖнӢ°н…Ңл„ҢнҠё мғҢл“ңл°•мҠӨ, YAML config нҲҙл§Ғ, н•ҷмҠөлҚ°мқҙн„° trajectory м••м¶•)лҠ” м ңн’Ҳ/л°°нҸ¬ нҳ•нғңлқј single-user лЎңм»¬ Museм—җ л§Өн•‘ м•Ҳ лҗЁ." лӢӨмқҢ мҠӨм№ҙмҡ°нҠёлҠ” лӢӨлҘё м¶•(мӢ к·ң л…јл¬ё, мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ н”„лЎңлёҢ, нҡҢк·Җ)мңјлЎң м „нҷҳ к¶ҢмһҘ.

parity/Muse-мҡ°мң„ нҷ•мқё(м•Ўм…ҳ м—ҶмқҢ): eval мқён”„лқј Muse мҡ°мң„, atomic write coreВ·failure taxonomyВ·circuit breaker parity, prompt cache_controlмқҖ лЎңм»¬ postureмғҒ мқҳлҸ„м Ғ non-gap.

## вҳ… capability-parity вҖ” hermes/openclaw лҢҖл№„ мҲңмҲҳ м—җмқҙм „нҠё м—ӯлҹү к°ӯ (2026-06-23 gap-scout, мҪ”л“ңл ҲлІЁ л№„көҗ)

Theme: MuseлҘј hermes/openclaw кёү peerлЎң. grounding/local н•ҙмһҗлҠ” floorлЎң мң м§Җн•ҳкі , л‘ҳ лӢӨ к°ҖмЎҢлҠ”лҚ° Museк°Җ м–Үкұ°лӮҳ м—ҶлҠ” **мҲңмҲҳ м—җмқҙм „нҠё м—ӯлҹү 4к°ң**лҘј кІ°м •лЎ -мҡ°м„ мңјлЎң л©”мҡҙлӢӨ. (мҶҢмҠӨ: /Users/jinan/ai/hermes-agent, /Users/jinan/ai/openclaw мҪ”л“ңл ҲлІЁ мқёлІӨнҶ лҰ¬.)

> рҹ“ҡ **кІҪмҹҒмӮ¬ teardown (к·ёл“Өмқҙ мӢӨм ңлЎң лӯҳ н•ҳлҠ”м§Җ)**: [`competitor-teardown.md`](competitor-teardown.md) вҖ” 2026-06-23 **20-н…Ңл§Ҳ exhaustive мҶҢмҠӨ л¶„м„қ + completeness critic**мқҙ openclaw/hermesлҘј **мӢӨм ң 420к°ң distinct нҢҢмқј м—ҙм–ҙ** мһ‘лҸҷл°©мӢқмқ„ н•ҙл¶Җ (260 capability, н…Ңл§Ҳлі„ л№„көҗ teardown + м•„нӮӨн…ҚмІҳ cross-cutting 8 + criticмқҙ лҶ“м№  л»”н•ң м—ӯлҹү 10). "мҷёл¶Җ кІҪмҹҒмӮ¬к°Җ лӯҳ н•ҳлҠ”м§Җ" мқҙн•ҙмҡ©.
>
> рҹ“Ӣ **м „мІҙ кё°нҡҢ м№ҙнғҲлЎңк·ё (231к°ң)**: [`capability-parity-backlog.md`](capability-parity-backlog.md) вҖ” мң„ teardownм—җм„ң лҸ„м¶ңн•ң Muse к°ңл°ң кё°нҡҢ. лӘЁл“  к·јкұ° нҢҢмқјкІҪлЎң кІҪмҹҒмӮ¬ л ҲнҸ¬ мӢӨмһ¬ кё°кі„кІҖмҰқ(нҸҗкё° 0), м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ© + Muse мһҗмІҙ кө¬нҳ„л°©мӢқ + verify кІҢмқҙнҠё. м•„лһҳ Gap 1вҖ“4лҠ” 1м°Ё м°©мҲҳ мҷ„лЈҢ мҠ¬лқјмқҙмҠӨ, лӮҳлЁём§ҖлҠ” м№ҙнғҲлЎңк·ём—җм„ң вҳ… мҡ°м„ мҲңмң„лЎң н”Ҫ.
>
> вҡ–пёҸ **Muse-м Ғн•© мӢ¬мӮ¬ (231к°ң лҸ…лҰҪнҢҗм •)**: [`capability-parity-judgment.md`](capability-parity-judgment.md) вҖ” build 121 / maybe 59 / skip 51 (off-strategy 50 = л©ҖнӢ°н…Ңл„ҢнҠёВ·нҒҙлқјмҡ°л“ңВ·мұ„л„җмҠӨн”„лЎӨмқҖ лӢЁмқјмӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ лЎңм»¬ Museм—җ л¶Җм Ғн•©). л№Ңл“ң м°©мҲҳлҠ” м—¬кё° buildВ·coreВ·strengthens н•ӯлӘ©л¶Җн„°.

### вң… л№Ңл“ң м°©мҲҳ вҖ” capability-parity build (build нҒҗм—җм„ң мҲңм°Ё м§„н–ү)

- вң… **кІ°м •лЎ м Ғ tool-result мҡ”м•Ҫмқ„ truncation л§Ҳм»Өм—җ м Ғмһ¬** (CMP: deterministic pre-LLM tool-result summarization) вҖ” `d6ffa8997`. мһҳлҰ° лҸ„кө¬кІ°кіјк°Җ `[truncated вҖҰ]` лҢҖмӢ  мҪ”л“ңмң лҸ„ 1мӨ„ мҡ”м•Ҫ(`terminal: exit 0 В· 120 lines`, `search: 37 results`)мқ„ ліҙм—¬мӨҢ вҶ’ "shows its work" к°•нҷ”. `@muse/memory` мҲңмҲҳн•ЁмҲҳ `summarizeToolResult`(нҶ нҒ°лӢЁмң„ л¶„лҘҳ) + `capToolOutput` л°°м„ ; 12 unit + 2 wiring н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified, lint 0. hermes `context_compressor.py` нҢЁн„ҙ м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **envelope-aware нҶ нҒ° м№ҙмҡҙнҢ…** (CMP: envelope-aware token budget) вҖ” `b5aad64e4`. `estimateMessageTokens`к°Җ лі‘л ¬ tool нҳём¶ң Nк°ңлҘј message overhead 1к°ңлЎң кіјмҶҢкі„мғҒн•ҳлҚҳ лІ„к·ё мҲҳм • вҖ” tool нҳём¶ң/кІ°кіјл§ҲлӢӨ wire-envelope 8нҶ нҒ° л¶Җкіј вҶ’ л©ҖнӢ°нҲҙ н„ҙ мҳҲмӮ° м •м§Ғ кі„мғҒ, нҠёлҰј м Ғкё° л°ңлҸҷ(silent overflow л°©м§Җ). л§Өм§ҒлІ„м§“ н…ҢмҠӨнҠё 1к°ң мһ¬көҗм •(97вҶ’113=trio мӢӨм ңнҒ¬кё°) + delta н…ҢмҠӨнҠё 2к°ң; mutation-verified; @muse/memory 599 + @muse/agent-core 2623 green, lint 0. hermes `context_compressor.py` м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **кІ°м •лЎ м Ғ м—җлҹ¬ л¶„лҘҳкё° + кё°ліё retry м •мұ…** (REL: error taxonomy) вҖ” `751dbe68a`. `classifyError`к°Җ мһ„мқҳ м—җлҹ¬лҘј нҡҢліө-кҙҖл Ё л¶„лҘҳ(auth/rate_limit/overloaded/server_error/timeout/network/context_overflow/content_policy/model_not_found/bad_request/unknown) + recovery hintsлЎң кІ°м •лЎ  л§Өн•‘(HTTP status+л©”мӢңм§Җ нҢЁн„ҙ, LLM/IO м—ҶмқҢ). `retry()` кё°ліём •мұ…мңјлЎң л°°м„  вҶ’ лӘ…л°ұ мҳҒкө¬м—җлҹ¬лҠ” мҰүмӢң fail-fast(м „м—” м „ attempt мҶҢм§„), transient/unknownмқҖ retryable мң м§Җ(кё°мЎҙ лҸҷмһ‘ ліҙмЎҙ), лӘ…мӢңм Ғ retryableмқҖ override. 12+2 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/resilience 38 + agent-core 2623 + scheduler 91 + autoconfigure 632 green, lint 0. hermes `error_classifier.py` м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вҸӯпёҸ **skill curator лқјмқҙн”„мӮ¬мқҙнҒҙ** вҖ” already-covered: @muse/skills `authored-skill-store.ts`к°Җ мқҙлҜё lastUsedAtВ·quarantineВ·auto-archive(stale)В·cap-by-archivingВ·restore ліҙмң  вҶ’ no-op нҡҢн”ј, л№Ңл“ң м•Ҳ н•Ё.
- вң… **м»ҙнҢ©м…ҳ мӢң stale мқёлқјмқё мқҙлҜём§Җ мҠӨнҠёлҰҪ** (CMP-2: media stripping) вҖ” `b83dac2a7`. л№„м „ н„ҙмқҳ multi-MB base64 мқҙлҜём§Җк°Җ л§Ө н„ҙ мһ¬м „мҶЎлҗҳлҚҳ л¬ём ң(м¶”м •кё° м№ҙмҡҙнҠёлҸ„ м•Ҳ лҗЁ) вҖ” `stripStaleImageAttachments`к°Җ л§Ҳм§Җл§ү user л©”мӢңм§Җ мқҙм „ н„ҙмқҳ мқёлқјмқё мқҙлҜём§Җ л°”мқҙнҠёлҘј м ңкұ°н•ҳкі  `[image omitted: <mime> ~<KB>]` н”Ңл ҲмқҙмҠӨнҷҖлҚ”лЎң лҢҖмІҙ(нҳ„мһ¬ н„ҙ мқҙлҜём§ҖВ·URL refмқҖ ліҙмЎҙ). `trimConversationMessages` кө¬мЎ° pre-passлЎң л°°м„ (л§Ө нҳём¶ң, boundary-integrityмІҳлҹј), no-op мӢң мӣҗліё л°ҳнҷҳ. 5 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/memory 604 + agent-core 2623 green, lint 0. openclaw/hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вҸӯпёҸ **м¶”к°Җ already-covered нҷ•мқё**: tool-call м •нҷ•м„ңлӘ… dedup(`ToolCallDeduplicator` ліҙмң , mutation-safe), dangerous-path/secret-file(`fs-path-safety.ts`), secret/PII redaction(`@muse/policy`), лӘЁмҲңнғҗм§Җ(`agent-core/contradiction-detection.ts`), leading think-strip(`provider-shared.ts`, мқҳлҸ„м Ғ leading-only) вҶ’ no-op нҡҢн”ј.
- вң… **classifierк°Җ мӨ‘мІ© provider м—җлҹ¬ unwrap** (REL-10: nested-metadata extraction) вҖ” `1f041825e`. classifyErrorк°Җ top-level `.message`л§Ң лҙҗм„ң лһҳн•‘лҗң м—җлҹ¬(OpenRouter `metadata.raw`=мғҒлҘҳ м—җлҹ¬ JSON л¬ёмһҗм—ҙ, OpenAI `{error:{message}}`)мқҳ мӢӨм ң мӣҗмқёмқ„ лӘ» лҙ„ вҶ’ лһҳн•‘лҗң rate-limit/context-overflowк°Җ `unknown` мҳӨл¶„лҘҳ. `extractMessage`к°Җ мӨ‘мІ© м—җлҹ¬ н…ҚмҠӨнҠёлҸ„ surface(join)н•ҙ reason нҢЁн„ҙмқҙ м§„м§ң м—җлҹ¬лҘј л§Өм№ӯ. л№„мӨ‘мІ©мқҖ byte-identical. 4 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/resilience 58 + agent-core 2630 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©. (BYO-cloud кІҪлЎң к°Җм№ҳ; local OllamaлҠ” л№„мӨ‘мІ©мқҙлқј л¬ҙмҳҒн–Ҙ.)
- вң… **лҲ„м¶ңлҗң grounding-fenceлҘј лӢөліҖ м¶ңл Ҙм—җм„ң мҠӨнҒ¬лҹҪ** (MEM-1: streaming context-fence scrub) вҖ” `f057851af`. gemma4к°Җ н”„лЎ¬н”„нҠёмқҳ grounding лё”лЎқ fence(`<<memory N>>`В·`<<note>>`В·`<<end>>`)лҘј лӢөліҖм—җ ECHOн•ҳл©ҙ лӮҙл¶Җ recall л№„кі„к°Җ мң м Җм—җкІҢ л…ём¶ңлҗЁ(мҠӨнҠёлҰ¬л°Қ citation кІҢмқҙнҠёлҠ” `[from]`/`[memory:]` мҳҒмҲҳмҰқл§Ң мҠӨнҒ¬лҹҪ, `<<вҖҰ>>` кІҪкі„лҠ” м•Ҳ н•Ё). `stripGroundingFences`(кІ°м •лЎ  м¶ңл Ҙмң„мғқ, н”„лЎ¬н”„нҠё м•„лӢҢ мҪ”л“ң; м •л°Җ л¬ёлІ•мңјлЎң `1 << 2`В·`cout << note`В·`<<TODO>>`лҠ” ліҙмЎҙ) м¶”к°Җ + `muse ask` мҠӨнҠёлҰјн‘ңмӢңВ·лІ„нҚјлӢөліҖ(citation кІҢмқҙнҠё м „) м–‘мӘҪ л°°м„  вҶ’ лҲ„м¶ң fenceк°Җ н„°лҜёл„җ/нһҲмҠӨнҶ лҰ¬/episodicм—җ м•Ҳ лӮЁмқҢ. 5 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/recall 500 + @muse/cli 3003 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **aux-model м••м¶• мҪ”м–ҙ н”„лҰ¬лҜёнӢ°лёҢ** (CMP-2 core) вҖ” `8aa3117e4`. м»ҙнҢ©м…ҳ мҡ”м•ҪмқҖ кІ°м •лЎ (`[Key details]` salient facts)мқҙ FLOOR. CMP-2лҠ” л“ңлЎӯлҗң л©”мӢңм§ҖлҘј к°’мӢј aux лӘЁлҚё(2м°Ё лЎңм»¬ Ollama)мқҙ мҡ”м•Ҫн•ҳлҠ” мҳөм…ҳ л Ҳмқҙм–ҙ м¶”к°Җ. мқҙлІҲм—” model-AGNOSTIC мҪ”м–ҙ н”„лҰ¬лҜёнӢ°лёҢ `summarizeDroppedContext(dropped, summarizer, {fallback, maxChars})` м¶ңн•ҳ вҖ” summarizer мЈјмһ…мӢқ(лІӨлҚ” SDK лҜём°ёмЎ°), throw/empty/л¬ҙ-summarizer/л¬ҙ-drop м „л¶Җ кІ°м •лЎ  fallbackмңјлЎң FAIL-OPEN(CMP-1 мӣҗм№ҷ, м»ҙнҢ©м…ҳ м ҲлҢҖ м•Ҳ л©Ҳм¶Ө). вҸӯпёҸ лҹ°нғҖмһ„ л°°м„ (sync prepareModelRequest м»ҙнҢ©м…ҳ м§Җм җм—җ async aux нҳём¶ң)мқҖ лӢӨмқҢ мҠ¬лқјмқҙмҠӨ(мқҳлҸ„м Ғ, hot-path async лҰ¬нҢ©н„°). 6 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/memory 617 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **нҠёлҰ¬лЁёк°Җ compacted-away л©”мӢңм§Җ л…ём¶ң** (CMP-2 enabler) вҖ” `e1a0c73c8`. CMP-2 aux мҡ”м•ҪмқҖ л“ңлЎӯлҗң л©”мӢңм§Җк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳлӮҳ trimмқҖ `removedCount`л§Ң ліҙкі н•ҙ нҳём¶ңл¶Җк°Җ лӢӨмӨ‘-pass trim л„ҲлЁёлЎң droppedлҘј мһ¬мң лҸ„н•ҙм•ј н–ҲмқҢ(м·Ём•Ҫ). `ConversationTrimResult.dropped`(мһ…л Ҙ мӨ‘ retained м§‘н•©м—җ м—ҶлҠ” л©”мӢңм§Җ, м°ёмЎ°-лҸҷл“ұ diff; kept-but-repairedлҠ” нҸ¬н•Ёлҗ  мҲҳ мһҲмңјлӮҳ мҡ”м•Ҫм—” л¬ҙн•ҙ) м¶”к°Җ, м»ҙнҢ©м…ҳ м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ л№Ҳ л°°м—ҙ. вҶ’ summarizeDroppedContextлҘј лҹ°нғҖмһ„м—җ л°°м„ н•  л•Ң нҳём¶ңл¶Җк°Җ diff мһ¬кө¬м„ұ л¶Ҳн•„мҡ”. additive(кё°мЎҙ мҶҢл№„мһҗ л¬ҙмҳҒн–Ҙ, agent-core 2630 green). 2 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified(predicate л°ҳм „вҶ’RED); @muse/memory 619 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0.
- вң… **CMP-2 лҹ°нғҖмһ„ л°°м„  (CMP-2 COMPLETE)** вҖ” `75760bec1`. н”„лҰ¬лҜёнӢ°лёҢ+dropped-л…ём¶ңмқ„ лҹ°нғҖмһ„мқҙ мӢӨм ң мӮ¬мҡ©. opt-in `AgentRuntimeOptions.contextSummarizer`(+`contextSummaryMaxChars` кё°ліё 600): м»ҙнҢ©м…ҳ л°ңмғқ н„ҙ(summaryInserted)м—җ л“ңлЎӯлҗң л©”мӢңм§ҖлҘј мЈјмһ… aux лӘЁлҚёмқҙ мҡ”м•ҪвҶ’`augmentCompactionSummary`к°Җ кІ°м •лЎ  `[Conversation summary вҖҰ]` лё”лЎқм—җ `[Dropped-context summary: вҖҰ]`лЎң APPEND(кІ°м •лЎ  [Key details] floor ліҙмЎҙ, auxлҠ” лқјлІЁлҗң м¶”к°Җл¶„). л№„нҳ‘мғҒ мӨҖмҲҳ: model-AGNOSTIC(summarizer мЈјмһ…), FAIL-OPEN(empty/errorвҶ’кІ°м •лЎ  мҡ”м•Ҫ к·ёлҢҖлЎң), OPT-IN(лҜём„Өм •вҶ’aux нҳём¶ң м—ҶмқҢвҶ’кё°мЎҙ 2630 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё byte-identical). 5 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё(3 pure + 2 wired-integration through AgentRuntime.run w/ capturing provider), mutation-verified(helper append м ңкұ°вҶ’pure+wired RED); @muse/agent-core 2635 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. вҸӯпёҸ CLI/м„ңлІ„к°Җ лЎңм»¬ Ollama aux summarizerлҘј мЈјмһ…н•ҳл©ҙ мӢӨмӮ¬мҡ© нҷңм„ұнҷ”(м–ҙлҢ‘н„° wiringмқҖ нӣ„мҶҚ).
- вң… **CMP-2 мӢӨмӮ¬мҡ© нҷңм„ұнҷ” (assembled runtime, opt-in) вҖ” CMP-2 м „л¶Җ мҷ„лЈҢ** вҖ” `8ac5a49fb`. `createModelDroppedContextSummarizer`(Muse `ModelProvider` м¶”мғҒвҶ’`DroppedContextSummarizer`, к°ҷмқҖ лЎңм»¬лӘЁлҚё 2м°Ё нҳём¶ңлЎң л“ңлЎӯлҗң н„ҙ мҡ”м•Ҫ)лҘј autoconfigureк°Җ `MUSE_AUX_COMPACTION` мјңм§Ҳ л•Ң лҹ°нғҖмһ„ contextSummarizerлЎң мЈјмһ…. кё°ліё OFF(м»ҙнҢ©м…ҳ н„ҙ м¶”к°Җ нҳём¶ң м§Җм—°). л№„нҳ‘мғҒ: model-AGNOSTIC(нҢ©нҶ лҰ¬к°Җ ModelProvider л°ӣмқҢ, лІӨлҚ” SDK м•„лӢҳ; CLIк°Җ лЎңм»¬ Ollama мЈјмһ…), fail-openмқҖ summarizeDroppedContextм—җ(provider throwвҶ’кІ°м •лЎ  fallback), opt-in default-offвҶ’autoconfigure 632 л¬ҙліҖ. 3 нҢ©нҶ лҰ¬ н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified(transcript м ңкұ°вҶ’RED); @muse/agent-core 2638 + @muse/autoconfigure 632 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. **CMP-2 4мҠ¬лқјмқҙмҠӨ е®Ң: н”„лҰ¬лҜёнӢ°лёҢ+droppedл…ём¶ң+лҹ°нғҖмһ„л°°м„ +нҷңм„ұнҷ”.**
- вң… **run_command нҢҢкөӯ лӘ…л № fail-close к°Җл“ң** (TX-6, MuseмӢқ=кұ°л¶Җ) вҖ” `0f56a84c3`. run_commandлҠ” risk:execute(мҠ№мқё кІҢмқҙнҠё)м§Җл§Ң auto-approve/мһҗмңЁ лӘЁл“ңк°Җ кІҢмқҙнҠёлҘј мҡ°нҡҢн•  мҲҳ мһҲкі , мқјл¶Җ лӘ…л №мқҖ л№„к°Җм—ӯмқҙлқј лӘЁлҚё нҢҗлӢЁл§ҢмңјлЎң м ҲлҢҖ мӢӨн–ү л¶Ҳк°Җм—¬м•ј н•Ё. `classifyDangerousCommand`к°Җ мўҒкі  лӘ…нҷ•н•ң нҢҢкөӯ м§‘н•©(лЈЁнҠё/нҷҲ/лЈЁнҠёкёҖлЎӯ мһ¬к·ҖмӮӯм ңВ·fork bombВ·raw-device dd/redirectВ·mkfsВ·wipefs)мқ„ кІ°м •лЎ  нғҗм§Җ, `parseRunnerCommandRequest`к°Җ runner нҳём¶ң м „м—җ мҪ”л“ңм—җм„ң кұ°л¶Җ(fail-close, "к°Җл“ңлҠ” кІ°м •лЎ  мҪ”л“ң"). мҳӨнғҗ л°©м§ҖлЎң лІ”мң„ нғҖмқҙнҠё: мғҒлҢҖкІҪлЎң `rm -rf ./build`В·`ls /`В·`cat /etc/hosts`В·мқҙлҜём§Җк°„ ddлҠ” нҶөкіј(нҸүмҶҢ execute мҠ№мқё кІҢмқҙнҠёлЎң). command+args л¶„лҰ¬нҳ•лҸ„ full-line мһ¬кө¬м„ұмңјлЎң нғҗм§Җ. 9 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified(л¶„лҘҳкё° л¬ҙл Ҙнҷ”вҶ’RED); @muse/tools 306 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **м„ём…ҳ crash-detection л§Ҳм»Ө** (SES-3/10 foundation) вҖ” `01d9467a9`. мұ— м„ём…ҳ н„ҙмқҖ END-of-session нҢҢмқҙн”„лқјмқём—җм„ң мһҘкё°кё°м–өмңјлЎң flushлҗҳлҠ”лҚ° н”„лЎңм„ёмҠӨк°Җ лЁјм Җ мЈҪмңјл©ҙ flush м•Ҳ лҸј н„ҙ мң мӢӨ. `markSessionStart`(л¶ҖнҢ… мӢң atomic л§Ҳм»Ө)В·`markSessionCleanExit`(м •мғҒ мў…лЈҢ мӢң м ңкұ°)В·`detectUncleanShutdown`(л§Ҳм»Ө мһ”мЎҙ=м§Ғм „ нҒ¬лһҳмӢң вҶ’ нҳём¶ңл¶Җк°Җ мң мӢӨ н„ҙ ліөкө¬ к°ҖлҠҘ). atomic write(half-marker мҶҗмғҒ л°©м§Җ)В·кІ°м •лЎ В·corrupt/missingвҶ’clean. 5 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified(clean-exit no-opвҶ’RED); @muse/stores 354 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. вҸӯпёҸ CLI лқјмқҙн”„мӮ¬мқҙнҒҙ л°°м„ мқҖ нӣ„мҶҚ(мұ— л¶ҖнҢ…/мў…лЈҢ кІҪлЎң, мӢ мӨ‘ мҡ”). hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **SES л§Ҳм»ӨлҘј мұ— REPL лқјмқҙн”„мӮ¬мқҙнҒҙм—җ л°°м„ ** (SES-3 wiring) вҖ” `481f602ab`. л§Ҳм»ӨлҘј мӢӨмӮ¬мҡ©нҷ”: REPL л¶ҖнҢ… мӢң `beginSessionWithCrashCheck`к°Җ м§Ғм „ м„ём…ҳ л§Ҳм»Ө мһ”мЎҙ(нҒҙлҰ° мў…лЈҢ м•Ҳ н•Ё=нҒ¬лһҳмӢң) нғҗм§Җ нӣ„ мқҙлІҲ start кё°лЎқ, нҒҙлҰ° мў…лЈҢ мӢң `endSessionClean` м ңкұ°. м§Ғм „ нҒ¬лһҳмӢң к°җм§Җ мӢң 1мӨ„ notice(н„ҙмқҖ last-chat.jsonlм—җ мқҙлҜё durableмқҙлқј м •ліҙм„ұ). detect-before-mark мҲңм„ң мң м§Җ. лқјмқҙн”„мӮ¬мқҙнҒҙ лЎңм§ҒмқҖ м–ҮмқҖ мЈјмһ… seam(session-recovery.ts)мңјлЎң Ink лҹ°нғҖмһ„ м—Ҷмқҙ лӢЁмң„н…ҢмҠӨнҠё; REPL нҳём¶ңмқҖ .catch-guarded(мқём ‘ appendSessionBoundary нҢЁн„ҙ). вҸӯпёҸ stranded н„ҙ re-flush ліөкө¬лҠ” нӣ„мҶҚ. 4 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified(нғҗм§Җ м ңкұ°вҶ’RED); @muse/cli 3007 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0.
- вң… **н…ҚмҠӨнҠём—җм„ң SSRF-м•Ҳм „ bare-URL м¶”м¶ң** (WEB-5) вҖ” `884431ee7`. web-url-guardлҠ” мЈјм–ҙм§„ URLл§Ң кІҖмҰқ(assertPublicHttpUrlSync), мһҗмң  н…ҚмҠӨнҠём—җм„ң URL м¶”м¶ңмқҖ м—Ҷм—ҲмқҢ. `extractPublicHttpUrls`к°Җ prose мҶҚ http(s) URL(л§ҲнҒ¬лӢӨмҡҙ л§ҒнҒ¬ нғҖк№ғ нҸ¬н•Ё, лӢ«лҠ” кҙ„нҳё/лҢҖкҙ„нҳём—җм„ң л©Ҳм¶Ө)мқ„ м°ҫм•„ лҒқ л¬ёмһҘл¶Җнҳё stripВ·мҲңм„ңліҙмЎҙ dedup нӣ„ SSRF к°Җл“ң нҶөкіјл¶„л§Ң мң м§Җ вҖ” мЈјмһ…лҗң `169.254.169.254` л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„° lureВ·localhostВ·non-httpлҠ” л“ңлЎӯ. мҲңмҲҳВ·лҸҷкё°(DNSз„Ў), кё°мЎҙ к°Җл“ң мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©(мӨ‘ліөX). 6 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified(н•„н„° мҡ°нҡҢвҶ’RED); @muse/domain-tools 781 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **н…ҚмҠӨнҠём—җм„ң мқҙлҜём§Җ мҶҢмҠӨ(URL+лЎңм»¬кІҪлЎң) м¶”м¶ң** (MED-12) вҖ” `d75ba283f`. `muse ask --image`лҠ” лӘ…мӢң кІҪлЎңл§Ң л°ӣмқҢ, н…ҚмҠӨнҠём—җм„ң мқҙлҜём§Җ ref м¶”м¶ң м—Ҷм—ҲмқҢ. `extractImageSources`к°Җ мқҙлҜём§Җ URL(SSRF-safe `extractPublicHttpUrls` мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©+мқҙлҜём§Җнҷ•мһҘмһҗ н•„н„°, loopback/metadata lure мһҗкІ©м—ҶмқҢ) + ліҙмҲҳм Ғ лЎңм»¬кІҪлЎң(`/`В·`~/`В·`./`В·`../` м ‘л‘җ + мқҙлҜём§Җнҷ•мһҘмһҗл§Ң, proseмқҳ л§Ё нҢҢмқјлӘ…мқҖ мІЁл¶ҖлЎң м•Ҳ лҙ„) л°ҳнҷҳ. мҲңмҲҳВ·лҸҷкё°В·FS лҜём ‘к·ј(нҳём¶ңл¶Җк°Җ fs-path-safetyлЎң кІҢмқҙнҠё нӣ„ лЎңл“ң). vision auto-route кё°л°ҳ. 6 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified(нҷ•мһҘмһҗ н•„н„° м ңкұ°вҶ’RED); @muse/domain-tools 787 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **кёҙ TTS н…ҚмҠӨнҠё л¬ёмһҘкІҪкі„ cap** (MED-2) вҖ” `ee7843a4a`. TTS м—”м§„м—җ л„ҳкё°лҠ” н…ҚмҠӨнҠё кёёмқҙ м ңн•ң м—Ҷм—ҲмқҢ вҖ” л©ҖнӢ°нҺҳмқҙм§Җ лӢөліҖ м „мІҙлҘј н•©м„ұ(лҠҗлҰјВ·л¬ҙмқҳлҜёВ·мҲҳл¶„ л¶„лҹү). `truncateForTts`к°Җ к°ҖлҠҘн•ҳл©ҙ л¬ёмһҘмў…кІ°(. ! ?) кІҪкі„, м•„лӢҲл©ҙ лӢЁм–ҙ кІҪкі„, м•„лӢҲл©ҙ hard cutмңјлЎң мһҗлҘҙкі  к°ҖмІӯ '(truncated)' нҒҗ м¶”к°Җ. мҲңмҲҳВ·л§һмңјл©ҙ byte-identical. synthesizeWithPersona+Fallbackм—җ л°°м„ (кё°ліё 8000мһҗ cap)вҶ’л Ҳм§ҖмҠӨнҠёлҰ¬к°Җ л¬ҙн•ң blob м „лӢ¬ м•Ҳ н•Ё, м§§мқҖ лӢөліҖ л¶ҲліҖ. 6 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified(cap л¬ҙл Ҙнҷ”вҶ’3 RED); @muse/voice 141 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **нҢҢкөӯ лӘ…л № к°Җл“ңм—җ лЈЁнҠё мһ¬к·Җ chmod/chown м¶”к°Җ** (TX-6 нҷ•мһҘ) вҖ” `2cacedcd9`. TX-6 нҢҢкөӯ м§‘н•© мҷ„м„ұ: лЈЁнҠё/нҷҲ нҠёлҰ¬(`/`В·`/*`В·`~`В·`$HOME`) лҢҖмғҒ `chmod -R`/`chown -R`лҸ„ `parseRunnerCommandRequest`м—җм„ң fail-close(rm/dd/mkfsмҷҖ н•Ёк»ҳ). world-writable/мҶҢмң к¶Ң мһ¬л°°м •лҗң мӢңмҠӨн…ң нҠёлҰ¬лҠ” sudo/SSH к№Ём§Җкі  мһ¬мӢӨн–үмңјлЎң ліөкө¬л¶Ҳк°Җ, лЈЁнҠём—” м •лӢ№н•ң м—җмқҙм „нҠё мҡ©лҸ„ м—ҶмқҢ. rm к·ңм№ҷкіј лҸҷмқј нғҖмқҙнҠё нғҖк№ғ: мғҒлҢҖ `chmod -R 755 ./dist`В·`chmod +x ./script.sh`В·`chown -R me ./project`лҠ” нҶөкіј(нҸүмҶҢ execute мҠ№мқё). 8 мӢ к·ң мјҖмқҙмҠӨ(sudo м ‘л‘җ нҸ¬н•Ё), mutation-verified(chmod к·ңм№ҷ м°ЁлӢЁвҶ’RED); @muse/tools 306 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.

- вң… **мҠӨмјҖмӨ„лҹ¬ мқјмӢңм •м§Җ kill-switch** (CRON) вҖ” `6577abd33`. мһҗмңЁ мҠӨмјҖмӨ„ л°ңнҷ”(н”„лЎңм•ЎнӢ°лёҢВ·л°ұк·ёлқјмҡҙл“ң cron)м—җ лҢҖн•ң мң м Җ kill-switch, learning-pause нҢЁн„ҙ лҜёлҹ¬. `scheduler-pause-store`(`~/.muse/scheduler-paused.json`, corruptмӢң fail-open) + `DynamicScheduler`мқҳ мҳөм…ҳ `isPaused()` кІҢмқҙнҠёк°Җ cron-л°ңнҷ” runмқҖ мқјмӢңм •м§ҖмӨ‘ skipн•ҳлҗҳ мҲҳлҸҷ triggerлҠ” мӢӨн–ү(лӘ…мӢң мқҳлҸ„ мҡ°м„ ; мғҲ `automatic` н”Ңлһҳк·ёлЎң кө¬л¶„, м—¬кё°м„ң dryRunмқҖ preview мқҳлҜё). opt-in(лҜём„Өм •вҶ’never pausedвҶ’byte-identical). 4 store + 3 кІҢмқҙнҠё н…ҢмҠӨнҠё(мҪңл°ұ-л°ңнҷ” fake), л‘ҳ лӢӨ mutation-verified; @muse/scheduler 101 + @muse/stores 384 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.

- вҸӯпёҸ **мқҙлІҲ fire м¶”к°Җ already-covered**: no-progress лЈЁн”„к°җм§Җ(`ToolLoopProgressTracker.stalled()` + tool-failure-streak), per-subagent мҳҲмӮ°(к°Ғ workerк°Җ AgentRuntime maxToolCalls run + MAX_SUBTASKS), 3-tier н”„лЎ¬н”„нҠё/stable-prefix(`@muse/prompts` stable/dynamic section + stablePrefix + priority). **вҡ  SAFE лЎңм»¬-fit нҒҗ мӮ¬мӢӨмғҒ мҶҢм§„** вҖ” лӮЁмқҖ кі к°Җм№ҳлҠ” deferred(aux-model м••м¶•В·session мғҒнғңлЁёмӢ В·background-process л Ҳм§ҖмҠӨнҠёлҰ¬)лЎң attended лҰ¬л·° н•„мҡ”.
- вң… **ліөкө¬лҗң tool-argsмқҳ lone UTF-16 surrogate м •нҷ”** (TCR-3: surrogate sanitization) вҖ” `0fd28e48e`. л°”мқҙнҠёл ҲлІЁ лЎңм»¬лӘЁлҚёмқҙ лҜёмҢҚ surrogate(lone high/low)лҘј tool-argм—җ нқҳлҰ¬л©ҙ JSON.parseлҠ” нҶөкіјн•ҳлӮҳ downstream UTF-8 мқёмҪ”л”©(fetch body/мһ¬м „мҶЎ) мҶҗмғҒВ·лӢӨмқҢ provider кұ°л¶Җ. `sanitizeLoneSurrogates`(pairing-aware: м§„м§ң мқҙлӘЁм§Җ мҢҚ ліҙмЎҙ, surrogate м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ byte-identical) м¶”к°Җ + `recoverToolArgsJson`мқҙ ліөкө¬к°қмІҙмқҳ лӘЁл“  л¬ёмһҗм—ҙ нӮӨ/к°’мқ„ deep-walkн•ҙ U+FFFDлЎң м •нҷ”. 8 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/model 395 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. hermes `message_sanitization` м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **grounding-block fence лқјлІЁ мң„мЎ°л°©м§Җ** (provenance integrity, deferredм—җм„ң м•Ҳм „нҷ”) вҖ” `e00d30882`. к·ёлқјмҡҙл”© лё”лЎқ л№ҢлҚ”к°Җ memory KEY(+contact id)лҘј fence н—ӨлҚ”(`<<memory N вҖ” KEY>>`В·`[memory: KEY]`)мҷҖ renderMemoryFact topicм—җ UNescaped мӮҪмһ… вҶ’ мҳӨм—ј/auto-extractлҗң нӮӨк°Җ newline+`<<end>>`лЎң fence кІҪкі„ мң„мЎ° + к°Җм§ң grounded н•ӯлӘ© мЈјмһ… к°ҖлҠҘ(GROUNDEDвү TRUE кө¬л©Қ). `sanitizeFenceLabel`(control/newline/DEL/angle-bracketл§Ң м ңкұ°; мӢӨмӢқлі„мһҗм—” м—ҶлҠ” л¬ёмһҗ) м¶”к°ҖВ·м Ғмҡ©. м •мғҒ нӮӨлҠ” byte-identical, citation кІҢмқҙнҠёлҠ” token-overlapмқҙлқј м •лӢ№ мқёмҡ© л¶Ҳм•Ҫнҷ”. 3 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/recall 495 + byte-hygiene 45 green, lint 0. grounding м—Јм§Җ к°•нҷ”. (мқҙм „м—җ sensitiveлЎң ліҙлҘҳн–ҲмңјлӮҳ token-overlap л§Өм№ӯ нҷ•мқёмңјлЎң м•Ҳм „ мһ…мҰқ.)
- вң… **URL мҝјлҰ¬нҢҢлқјлҜён„° мӢңнҒ¬лҰҝ лҰ¬лҢҒм…ҳ** (SEC-1: url credential redaction) вҖ” `26ae28d90`. `redactSecretsInText`к°Җ userinfoВ·лІӨлҚ”нҶ нҒ° нҳ•нғңлҠ” мһЎм•ҳм§Җл§Ң мҝјлҰ¬нҢҢлқјлҜён„° VALUEлЎң мӢӨлҰ° мӢңнҒ¬лҰҝ(presigned `?X-Amz-Signature=`, мқјл°ҳ `?api_key=`/`?access_token=`/`?token=`)мқҖ к°’мқҙ м•Ңл Өм§„ нҳ•нғңк°Җ м•„лӢҲл©ҙ нҶөкіј вҶ’ лЎңк·ёВ·proactiveВ·л©”лӘЁлҰ¬В·toolм¶ңл Ҙм—җ лҲ„м¶ң. лҜјк°җ KEY л§Өм№ӯ нӣ„ к°’ лҰ¬лҢҒм…ҳ(к°ҖліҖкёёмқҙ lookbehindлЎң paramлӘ… ліҙмЎҙ). additive(лҰ¬лҢҒм…ҳл§Ң м¶”к°Җ), redactSecretsInTextм—җ н•©лҘҳлҸј лӘЁл“  нҳём¶ңмІҳм—җм„ң мҰүмӢң м Ғмҡ©. 1 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/shared 45 + agent-core 2630 green, lint 0. hermes/openclaw м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- рҹ”§ **byte-hygiene нҡҢк·Җ мҲҳм •** вҖ” `7250b9c19`. м—җмқҙм „нҠёмғқм„ұ competitor-teardown.mdмқҳ NULл°”мқҙнҠё(U+0000)к°Җ @muse/shared repo-byte-hygiene кІҢмқҙнҠё(goal-227) мң„л°ҳ вҶ’ `+`лЎң м№ҳнҷҳ, 45 green ліөкө¬. (мқҙлІҲ fireлҠ” нҡҢк·ҖмҲҳм • мҡ°м„  + SEC-1 лҸҷл°ҳ.)
- вң… **н„°лҜёл„җ л°°кІҪ к°җм§Җ + dim лҢҖл№„ к°Җл“ң** (UX-3: terminal theme/contrast) вҖ” `5c0fc7cd9`. CLI мғүм¶ңл Ҙмқҙ NO_COLOR/TTYлҠ” ліҙм§Җл§Ң л°°кІҪмқ„ л¬ҙмӢң вҶ’ лқјмқҙнҠё н…Ңл§Ҳм—җм„ң `dim`(нҡҢмғү)мқҙ кұ°мқҳ м•Ҳ ліҙмһ„. `detectTerminalBackground`(COLORFGBG нҢҢмӢұ: rxvt fg;;bg нҸ¬н•Ё, л§Ҳм§Җл§ү н•„л“ң=л°°кІҪ, 7/9-15=lightВ·0-6/8=dark) м¶”к°Җ + colorizeк°Җ KNOWN light л°°кІҪм—җм„  dimмқ„ нҸүл¬ёмңјлЎң. additive(COLORFGBG м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ unknownвҶ’byte-identical, dimл§Ң мҳҒн–Ҙ). 8 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/cli 3003 green, lint 0. openclaw м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **мӣ№кІҖмғү кІ°кіј canonical-URL л””л‘Ў** (WEB: search result dedup) вҖ” `c4fa62149`. DDG HTMLмқҙ к°ҷмқҖ URLмқ„ л°ҳліө вҶ’ parseDuckDuckGoHtmlмқҙ мӣҗмӢң л§Өм№ҳлҘј maxлЎң мһҳлқј мӨ‘ліөмқҙ кІ°кіј мҠ¬лЎҜ м°Ём§Җ(лЎңм»¬лӘЁлҚё м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё лӮӯл№„). мқҙм ң м „мІҙ мҲҳм§‘вҶ’canonical URL(host мҶҢл¬ёмһҗВ·fragment/trailing-slash м ңкұ°В·path+query ліҙмЎҙмңјлЎң ?id=1вү ?id=2)лЎң л””л‘ЎвҶ’max м»· = maxк°ң distinct. searxng кІҪлЎңлҸ„ лҸҷмқј м Ғмҡ©. 3 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/domain-tools 775 green, lint 0. openclaw/hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©. (WEB-1 н’Җ л©ҖнӢ°нҒҙлқјмҡ°л“ң л Ҳм§ҖмҠӨнҠёлҰ¬лҠ” лЎңм»¬-firstм—җ sprawlмқҙлқј лҜёмұ„нғқ; searxngвҶ’ddg нҸҙл°ұмңјлЎң мқҙлҜё м¶©л¶„.)
- вң… **TTS нҺҳлҘҙмҶҢлӮҳ л Ҳмқҙм–ҙ(мҡ”мІӯ мҡ°м„  precedence)** (MED-2: TTS persona) вҖ” `d79acb810`. ліҙмқҙмҠӨм—җ per-provider defaultVoice + per-request overrideл§Ң мһҲкі  мқјкҙҖлҗң "Muse лӘ©мҶҢлҰ¬" нҺҳлҘҙмҶҢлӮҳ м—ҶмқҢ. `TtsPersona`(provider+voice/format/speed кё°ліёк°’) + мҲңмҲҳ `resolveTtsPersona`(per-call н•„л“ңк°Җ н•ӯмғҒ мҡ°м„ , нҺҳлҘҙмҶҢлӮҳлҠ” л№Ҳм№ёл§Ң мұ„мӣҖ) + registry `synthesizeWithPersona`(нҺҳлҘҙмҶҢлӮҳк°Җ provider м„ нғқ, м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ primary). кІ°м •лЎ В·local-first. 7 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/voice 130 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©. CLI мұ„нғқмқҖ нӣ„мҶҚ.
- вң… **cron мһЎ retryм—җ мҳҒкө¬м—җлҹ¬ fail-fast** (CRON-1: error-classified cron retry) вҖ” `9fb488208`. мҠӨмјҖмӨ„лҹ¬ dispatch retry лЈЁн”„к°Җ лӘЁл“  мӢӨнҢЁлҘј maxRetryCountл§ҢнҒј л§№лӘ© мһ¬мӢңлҸ„(кі м • л”ңл Ҳмқҙ) вҶ’ мҳҒкө¬м—җлҹ¬(мһҳлӘ»лҗң toolлӘ…В·model-not-foundВ·authВ·кІҖмҰқ)лҸ„ м „ attempt мҶҢм§„. мқҙм ң catchл§ҲлӢӨ `ErrorClassifier`(@muse/resilience)лЎң л¶„лҘҳ вҶ’ мҳҒкө¬м—җлҹ¬лҠ” мҰүмӢң break, transient/unknownмқҖ кё°мЎҙлҢҖлЎң лҒқк№Ңм§Җ мһ¬мӢңлҸ„. м•һм„ң м¶ңн•ҳн•ң classifier мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©. 2 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё(мҳҒкө¬вҶ’1нҡҢ/transientвҶ’н’Җм№ҙмҡҙнҠё), mutation-verified; @muse/scheduler 93 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вҸӯпёҸ **already-covered (мқҙлІҲ fire)**: cron мһ¬м§„мһ… к°Җл“ң(scheduler-locks "another instance holds lock" skip), retry мқён”„лқј(retryOnFailure/maxRetryCount/retryDelayMs), лӘЁлҚёID tag ліҙмЎҙ(parseModelName), recall лӢӨм–‘м„ұ(hybrid-MMR=MEM-7 к°ңл…җdedup лҢҖмІҙ). вҡ ліҙлҘҳ: SES-* м„ём…ҳмғҒнғңлЁёмӢ /нҒ¬лһҳмӢңліөкө¬(hermes кІҢмқҙнҠёмӣЁмқҙ л©ҖнӢ°м„ём…ҳ кё°лҠҘ, лЎңм»¬ лӢЁмқјмӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ fit мқҳл¬ё), PRV-2/3 м№ҙнғҲлЎңк·ёВ·нҒҙлқјмҡ°л“ң failover(лЎңм»¬ fit лӮ®мқҢ).
- вң… **мҡ”мІӯ нҒ¬кё° л№„лЎҖ лӘЁлҚёмҪң нғҖмһ„м•„мӣғ** (PRV-10: request-scaled timeout) вҖ” `f3d91d36c`. лӘЁлҚёмҪң нғҖмһ„м•„мӣғмқҙ мҡ”мІӯ нҒ¬кё°мҷҖ л¬ҙкҙҖн•ҳкІҢ кі м • 120s вҶ’ нҒ° м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠёмқҳ м •лӢ№н•ҳкІҢ-лҠҗлҰ° лЎңм»¬ мғқм„ұмқҙ мӨ‘лҸ„ killлҗЁ. `scaleRequestTimeout(base, tokens)`к°Җ нҒ° мҡ”мІӯм—җ н•ңн•ҙ мғҒн–Ҙ(base*м¶”м •, 10л¶„ мәЎ), мһ‘мқҖ мҡ”мІӯмқҖ base мң м§Җ(byte-identical), base<=0(нғҖмһ„м•„мӣғ м—ҶмқҢ кҙҖлЎҖ) нҶөкіј. model-invocation нғҖмһ„м•„мӣғ seamм—җ char/4 м¶”м •мңјлЎң л°°м„ . 6 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/resilience 50 + agent-core 2630 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **кІ°м •лЎ м Ғ tool-call мӮ¬м „мӢӨн–ү лҜёл“ӨмӣЁм–ҙ(veto кІҢмқҙнҠё)** (TX-9: tool pre-call middleware) вҖ” `5a77e1374`. beforeTool нӣ…мқҖ кҙҖм°°м „мҡ©(л°ҳнҷҳ л¬ҙмӢң)мқҙлқј мӢӨн–ү м „ лҸ„кө¬нҳём¶ңмқ„ м •мұ…мңјлЎң л§үмқ„ seamмқҙ м—Ҷм—ҲмқҢ. `ToolCallMiddleware` мІҙмқёмқҙ мӢӨн–ү м§Ғм „ нҳём¶ңмқ„ veto к°ҖлҠҘ(мқҙмң лҠ” лӘЁлҚём—җ tool resultлЎң л…ём¶ң; мҳҲ: м ңн•ң м„ңлёҢм—җмқҙм „нҠё tool allowlist, нҢҢкҙҙм Ғ лҸ„кө¬ кёҲм§Җ). block-only(arg мһ¬мһ‘м„ұмқҖ dedupм„ңлӘ…В·conflictк°Җл“ң desync) + empty-default byte-identical(2628 лІ мқҙмҠӨлқјмқё л¶ҲліҖ). AgentRuntime мҳөм…ҳвҶ’runnerвҶ’per-call кІҢмқҙнҠё, кё°мЎҙ blockedToolResult кІҪлЎң н•©лҘҳ. 5 unit+2 wiring н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/agent-core 2630 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вҸӯпёҸ **м¶”к°Җ already-covered (мқҙлІҲ fire мЎ°мӮ¬)**: л©”мӢңм§Җ мӢңнҖҖмҠӨ/orphan-pair ліөкө¬(`memory-token-trim` ensureBoundaryIntegrity/removeOrphan*к°Җ л§Ө trim нҳём¶ң л¬ҙмЎ°кұҙ мӢӨн–ү), tool-arg к°•м ңліҖнҷҳ(`coerceToolArguments`/`coerceEnumArguments`/`groundToolArguments`), лӘЁлҚёID м •к·ңнҷ”(`parseModelName`), leading think-strip(мқҳлҸ„м Ғ leading-only). вҡ ліҙлҘҳ(лҜјк°җ/нҒ°): MEM-2 м¶ңл Ҙ fence-scrub(citation кІҢмқҙнҠё м •нҷ•м„ұ мң„н—ҳВ·CLI лӢөліҖкІҪлЎң), grounding-block key forgery л°©м§Җ(citation copy-exact мҡ”кө¬лЎң мң„н—ҳ), CMP-1 aux-model compression(м»ҙнҢ©м…ҳ кІҪлЎң LLMнҳём¶ңВ·көҗм°Ём ҲлӢЁ). attended лҰ¬л·° к¶ҢмһҘ.
- вң… **server-advised retry-after л°ұмҳӨн”„ мӨҖмҲҳ** (REL: rate-limit-aware backoff) вҖ” `12858334c`. `classifyError`м—җ кІ°м •лЎ м Ғ `retryAfterMs` м¶”м¶ң м¶”к°Җ(retryAfter/retry_after(мҙҲ)В·retryAfterMs(ms) н•„л“ң, `retry-after` н—ӨлҚ”(к°қмІҙ/get()/Map), л©”мӢңм§Җ нҢЁн„ҙ "try again in 2s"/"resets in 3m"/"wait 500ms"). `retry()`к°Җ retry-after мһҲмңјл©ҙ лё”лқјмқёл“ң м§ҖмҲҳл°ұмҳӨн”„ лҢҖмӢ  к·ё мӢңк°„л§ҢнҒј лҢҖкё°(maxDelayMs лҳҗлҠ” 60sлЎң мәЎ вҶ’ л№„м •мғҒк°’ н–ү л°©м§Җ), м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ кё°мЎҙ лҸҷмһ‘. rate-limited н”„лЎңл°”мқҙлҚ”лҘј мҡ”мІӯн•ң мңҲлҸ„мҡ°л§ҢнҒјл§Ң л°ұмҳӨн”„. 6 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/resilience 44 + agent-core 2623 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.
- вң… **м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё-мңҲлҸ„мҡ° мҠӨмјҖмқј tool-output мҳҲмӮ°** (REL-6: context-scaled budget) вҖ” `49353323b`. per-tool мәЎмқҙ лӘЁлҚё мңҲлҸ„мҡ°мҷҖ л¬ҙкҙҖн•ҳкІҢ кі м • 8kмҳҖмқҢ(мһ‘мқҖ лЎңм»¬ мңҲлҸ„мҡ°лҘј н•ң лІҲм—җ мӮјнӮҙ). `scaleToolOutputBudget(windowTokens, cap)`мқҙ мңҲлҸ„мҡ°мқҳ ~10%лЎң м¶•мҶҢ(м„Өм •к°’ мІңмһҘ м ҲлҢҖ м•Ҳ л„ҳк№ҖВ·floor ліҙмһҘВ·мңҲлҸ„мҡ° лҜёмғҒмқҙл©ҙ no-op). autoconfigureм—җм„ң мқҙлҜё кі„мӮ°лҗң contextWindowлЎң л°°м„ . 5 н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, mutation-verified; @muse/memory 609 + @muse/autoconfigure 632 green, lint 0. hermes м°ёмЎ°-м „мҡ©.

### Gap 1 вҖ” м—җмқҙм „нҠёк°Җ нҳём¶ң к°ҖлҠҘн•ң мһҗкё° кіјкұ° кІҖмғү (к°ҖмһҘ нҒ° к°ӯ; л‘ҳ лӢӨ мһҲкі  Museл§Ң м—ҶмқҢ)
hermes `session_search_tool.py`(FTS5 trigram, CJK), openclaw `memory-search.ts`(FTS5 + н•ҳмқҙлёҢлҰ¬л“ң BM25+vector+MMR). MuseлҠ” episodic recallмқҙ лӮҙл¶Җмҡ©мқј лҝҗ "м „м—җ X м–ҳкё°н•ң лҢҖнҷ”/л©”лӘЁ м°ҫм•„мӨҳ"лҘј м—җмқҙм „нҠёк°Җ нҳём¶ңн•  лҸ„кө¬к°Җ м—ҶмқҢ.
- вң“ S1 (fire 1): кІ°м •лЎ  CJK-aware lexical history-search мҪ”м–ҙ(`searchHistory` in @muse/recall, BM25). DONE.
- вң“ S2 (fire 2): мҪ”м–ҙлҘј м—җмқҙм „нҠё-нҳём¶ң лҸ„кө¬(`history_search`)лЎң л…ём¶ң + лҹ°нғҖмһ„ л Ҳм§ҖмҠӨнҠёлҰ¬ л°°м„  + eval:tools кіЁл“  мјҖмқҙмҠӨ. DONE.
- вң“ S3 (fire 6): н•ҳмқҙлёҢлҰ¬л“ң(lexical BM25 RRF + cosine) лһӯнӮ№ вҖ” `searchHistoryHybrid` in @muse/recall (queryVector+record embeddings мһҲмңјл©ҙ л‘җ лһӯнҒ¬лҰ¬мҠӨнҠёлҘј fuseByReciprocalRankлЎң fusion, м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ byte-identical lexical fallback; minCosine floorлЎң precision ліҙмЎҙ, л‘ҳ лӢӨ лӘ» л§һм¶”л©ҙ л№Ҳ кІ°кіј=fabrication 0). 9 OUTCOME vitest(нҢҢлқјн”„л ҲмқҙмҰҲк°Җ lexicalмқҖ 0 hitмқёлҚ° hybridк°Җ surfacing) + 1мӨ„ mutation RED-confirmed. Opus в‘Јb PASS. вҖ” capability-parity fire 6

### Gap 2 вҖ” skill curator лқјмқҙн”„мӮ¬мқҙнҒҙ (нҳ„мһ¬ quarantineл§Ң мһҲмқҢ)

- в—Ұ S1: skill usage мӮ¬мқҙл“ңм№ҙ(use_countВ·last_activityВ·view_count) кІ°м •лЎ  store + vitest. MUTATION-FIRST.
- вң“ S2: staleвҶ’archive мһҗлҸҷм „мқҙ вҖ” DONE (freshness-guard 2026-06-27): `authored-skill-store.ts` has lastUsedAt + auto-archive(stale) + cap-by-archiving + restore (line 289), and the curator daemon runs periodic stale-skill auto-archive (`08827dd75`). The whole Gap-2 lifecycle (S1 usage sidecar / S2 stale-archive) is covered (cf. line 39).
- в—Ұ S3: мӨ‘ліө authored-skill consolidation(кІ№м№Ё нғҗм§ҖвҶ’umbrella лі‘н•© м ңм•Ҳ, draft-first, мһҗлҸҷ нҷңм„ұ кёҲм§Җ).

### Gap 3 вҖ” scheduled multi-phase dreaming + inert м—ӯлҹү л°°м„ 
openclaw 3-phase dreaming(Light/Deep/REM, temporal decay, health нҡҢліө). MuseлҠ” мЎ°к°Ғл§Ң мһҲкі  м„ём…ҳ-лҒқ нӣ… only + н•өмӢ¬ inert.
- в—Ұ S1 (к°ҖмһҘ л№ лҘё ROI, 2мӨ„кёү): ACT-R `recallActivation`мқ„ `StoreBackedEpisodicRecallProvider.resolve()`м—җ л°°м„ (`useActrRanking:true` м „лӢ¬) вҖ” мқҙлҜё н…ҢмҠӨнҠёлҗң н•ЁмҲҳк°Җ episodic лһӯнӮ№м—җ м•Ҳ м“°мһ„. OUTCOME кІҖмҰқ(лһӯнӮ№ ліҖнҷ”) + eval:multihop.
- в—Ұ S2: multi-hop recall default-ON нҸүк°Җ нӣ„ н”ҢлҰҪ(мқҙлҜё 40%вҶ’80% мёЎм •лҗЁ, MUSE_RECALL_SECOND_HOP) вҖ” eval:multihop pass^k нҷ•мқё нӣ„.
- в—Ұ S3: кІ°м •лЎ  consolidationмқ„ мҠӨмјҖмӨ„ daemon armмңјлЎң(м„ём…ҳ-лҒқ only вҶ’ мЈјкё°м Ғ), promotion/decay кІҢмқҙнҠё мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©. health-кё°л°ҳ нҡҢліө нҠёлҰ¬кұ°(openclaw нҢЁн„ҙ) м°Ёмҡ©.
- в—Ұ S4: background-review default-ON кІҖнҶ (MUSE_BACKGROUND_REVIEW_ENABLED) вҖ” fail-softВ·write-gatedл©ҙ н”ҢлҰҪ, pass^k.

### Gap 4 вҖ” sub-agent мҳӨмјҖмҠӨнҠёл Ҳмқҙм…ҳ лӮҙкө¬м„ұ (Ollama н•„мҡ” мҠ¬лқјмқҙмҠӨлҠ” л°•мҠӨ quietн•  л•Ң)
openclaw `subagent-registry.ts`(persistent run registryВ·async announce non-pollingВ·orphan recovery). Muse lead-worker+councilмқҖ in-memory, registry/announce/recovery м—ҶмқҢ.
- вң“ S1 (fire 3): persistent sub-agent run registry store(`SubAgentRunRegistry`, @muse/multi-agent) вҖ” live run lifecycle (run idВ·parentвҶ’childВ·statusВ·timeoutВ·heartbeatВ·stall detection), distinct from FINISHED-run-audit OrchestrationHistory; orphan-by-construction rejected, frozen records, pure detectStalled + markStalledAsTimedOut. 21 OUTCOME-state vitest, 2 mutations RED-confirmed. Opus в‘Јb PASS. вҖ” capability-parity fire 3
- вң“ S2 (fire 5): wire SubAgentRunRegistry into the LIVE MultiAgentOrchestrator (closes the inert-store risk fire 3 flagged) вҖ” a real run now registers parent + each child worker run and transitions them runningвҶ’completed/failed/timed-out end-to-end; also threaded into apps/api orchestrate routes + new GET /api/multi-agent/runs live surface. Opus в‘Јb PASS. вҖ” capability-parity fire 5
- вң“ S2b вҖ” capability-parity fire 8: deterministic orphan-recovery policy on SubAgentRunRegistry (`detectOrphaned` flags a running child whose parent reached a terminal status вҖ” incl. a child registered against an already-terminal parent вҖ” ignoring root runs + already-terminal children; `recoverOrphaned` transitions orphans to `failed` with finishedAt/error, distinct from heartbeat-stall `timed-out`, leaving unrelated running state untouched). 5 OUTCOME-state vitest, 1-line mutation RED-confirmed. Orchestrator wiring deliberately NOT added (parent-failure catch is unreachable for orphans: runSequential/runParallel swallow worker errors вҶ’ children always terminal before parent settles), so it ships as a tested defensive primitive for a future scheduled sweep. Opus в‘Јb PASS.

- вҳ… NEXT (multi-step EARLY-STOP вҖ” the no-tool-at-all variant; step-REPETITION now addressed fire 49): NOTE вҖ” fire 49's trace showed the dominant mode was REPETITION (re-read loop), now nudged. Original decomposition (dual-eval evidence fire 48):
  with Ollama up, BOTH harder multi-step evals FAIL via early-stop/repetition вҖ” `eval:multifile-fix` AND `eval:edit-run-verify` each ran `tools=[file_read]` then the 12B STOPPED without editing/running (the buggy fn left unchanged). The deterministic tool-call veins (fires 40-47: arg recovery, name sanitize, coercion, path/grep/run_command hints, not-exposed suggestion) are largely exhausted; early-stop is model-behavior and the dominant remaining blocker. The fix is the fire-12 action-completion re-prompt, but it is genuinely >1 fire and must NOT be rammed (fire-12: "not auto-fodder"; reflection-guard: a retry surface needs a calibrated verifier + no mis-fire). DECOMPOSED loop-sized sub-slices:
  - (48a) DETECTOR вҖ” the existing `isUnbackedActionClaim` = `requestsToolAction(query) && answerClaimsAction(answer) && !actionToolRan(toolNames)` does NOT cover early-stop (the model STOPS without CLAIMING done вҶ’ `answerClaimsAction` false). Need a precise `actionRequiredButNoneTaken(query, toolNames)` = `requestsToolAction(query) && !actionToolRan(toolNames)` (drops the claim requirement), built with a HEAVY adversarial FP corpus: answer-only/advice/read-only queries ("what does X do?", "summarize X", "read X") must NOT fire. Pure predicate, Ollama-free, mutation-first. The precision of `requestsToolAction` is the whole ballgame вҖ” measure its FP rate on real traces before any wiring.
  - (48b) CONSOLIDATE вҖ” `runResistingFalseDone` is currently wrapped around the run ONLY on the chat-repl path (fire 32); the eval/server path (AgentRuntime.run) has no re-prompt. Decide the architecture: move the bounded re-prompt INTO AgentRuntime.run and have chat-repl delegate (NO double re-prompt). reflection-guard registry already points at false-done-reprompt.ts (fire 45) вҖ” the wrapper stays, its call site moves. Touches the shared core loop (server+CLI) вҶ’ highest blast radius; do on a NON-main-merge fire with chat-repl regression tests.
  - (48c) WIRE + VALIDATE вҖ” wire (48a)'s detector into (48b)'s re-prompt (bounded 1, verifier = a write/execute tool ran after), then validate the eval delta with pass^k (kвүҘ3, both evals) now that Ollama is up. Ship only if eval improves AND the FP corpus stays clean AND Opus в‘Јb judge PASS.

- в—Ұ run_command `maxOutputBytes` is named BYTES but the tool slices with `.slice()` (UTF-16 code units), so a multi-byte (Korean/emoji) output under-counts vs the byte budget вҖ” pre-existing naming/semantic mismatch (noted computer-control fire 44). - вң“ run_command silent-truncation flag вҖ” computer-control fire 44: the run_command tool re-sliced output by the model's `maxOutputBytes` but kept `truncated` from the runner, so a cap that cut the log left `truncated=false` and the model read partial output as complete. - вң“ RESOLVED (agent-hardening fire 12, `2f62ee0f`): single-marker dependent decomposition вҖ” a request with ONE sequencing marker + a real cross-step dependency ("л…ёнҠёлҘј кІҖмғүн•ң л’Ө к·ё кІ°кіјлҘј мҡ”м•Ҫн•ҙмӨҳ") now fans out (was dropped to single-agent by the `sequencing >= 2` gate, starving the sequenced-threading). REMAINING (conservative under-fire, low priority): a sentence-INITIAL KO marker ("лЁјм Җ вҖҰн•ҳкі  к·ё кІ°кіјлҘј вҖҰ") leaves the marker at clause position 0 so the split yields 1 clause and the rule can't admit it вҖ” a future fire could add a leading-marker-aware split if real traffic shows the miss matters. - вң“ RESOLVED (agent-hardening fire 14, `4db07c35`): MARKER-LESS dependent two-step decomposition вҖ” the no-ordered-marker half of the MAST gap (fire 12 closed the single-marker half). ## вҳ… Open вҖ” Muse edge hardening (WIDENED loop theme, м§„м•Ҳ-directed 2026-06-20 after fire 8)

> **VEIN STATUS (core-hardening fire 11, honest exhaustion of CLEAN 1-fire core-edge slices THIS session).** Fires 1-10 shipped verified hardening across all 6 touched (pkg,kind): grounding-floor (agent-core injection Г—2), local-tool-calling (model Ollama-schema), orchestration (multi-agent re-synthesis), anti-fabrication (agent-core gate-total), memory-integrity (memory noop + recall source-conflict), outbound-safety (mcp consented-log) вҖ” plus 2 verifier-catches (fire 6 KO-injection 68% FP, fire 10 drill). NEXT high-value moves are DELIBERATE >1-fire decomposes or a retheme вҖ” м§„м•Ҳ to choose (pause / pick a decompose / retheme). Auto-firing will otherwise produce thin/exhaustion fires.

- вң“ (G1) **Surface the `source-conflict` weakness axis for remediation** вҖ” DONE (competitor-grounding fire 9, self-development): `source-conflict` (the user's OWN saved notes disagree вҖ” written to the ledger since fire 5 but read by NO selector) is now user-remediable: `USER_REMEDIABLE_AXES = {grounding-gap, source-conflict}` in `selectRemediableWeaknesses`, `RemediableWeakness` carries its `axis`, and new `remediationHint(axis, topic)` renders the DIFFERENT fix per axis ("add a note about X" vs "your saved notes about X disagree вҖ” reconcile them"). OUTCOME-verified end-to-end (a source-conflict ledger entry вҶ’ gatherEveningRecap вҶ’ reconcile copy, NOT "add a note") + Opus в‘Јb judge PASS 6/6 (verified EXHAUST: of the 7 axes, only 4 are production-WRITTEN and all 4 now read by a selector вҖ” source-conflict was the lone written-but-unread). - вң“ (G2) **Unify the injection neutralizers вҖ” give the live-surface neutralizer policy's evasion-decoding** вҖ” DONE (competitor-grounding fire 10, grounding-floor; this fire was also the JUDGE-DRILL). BOTH chokepoints now match against `@muse/policy`'s `normalizeForInjectionDetection` (entity-decode + NFKC + zero-width-strip + homoglyph-fold + diacritical-strip): `isMemoryInjection` (atomic facts) + `neutralizeInjectionSpans` (ALL tool/MCP/sub-agent output via capToolOutput + the two plan-execute paths + note/episode/feed prose). So a homoglyph-`С–gnore` / `&#105;gnore` injection in tool output / recall prose is now neutralized. KEY DESIGN: `neutralizeInjectionSpans` uses a clean-text FAST PATH вҖ” if the normalized form has no injection it returns the ORIGINAL byte-identical, so normalization's diacritical/NFKC collateral is paid ONLY on injection-containing (untrusted) text; clean accents/fullwidth recall content is never mangled. Judge verified NO fast-path false-negative (normalization only ADDS matchability for the ASCII patterns вҶ’ superset). OUTCOME-verified end-to-end (capToolOutput + note-chunk homoglyph neutralized; clean accented byte-identical) + Opus в‘Јb judge PASS 6/6. Closes T1-c-resid ii.
- вң“ (G3) **Per-fact provenance (firstSeen / lastConfirmed / confirmCount / freshness)** вҖ” DONE (competitor-grounding fire 11, memory-integrity). STALE-finding corrected: NO risky `facts`-store migration was needed вҖ” the per-fact provenance DATA already exists in the append-only `BeliefProvenance` log (`@muse/memory/belief-provenance-store.ts`: `learnedAt` written on every learn, by auto-extract + `muse memory set`). New `deriveFactProvenance(entries)` aggregates the log per key вҶ’ `{firstSeen=min, lastConfirmed=max, confirmCount, source=user-outranks-auto, value=at-latest}`; new `classifyFactFreshness({lastConfirmed,now,agingDays=30,staleDays=90})` вҶ’ fresh/aging/stale. - вң“ (G4) **Memory-promotion gate вҖ” durable user-fact promotion from gated recurrent confirmation** вҖ” DONE (competitor-grounding fire 12, memory-integrity). New `selectPromotableFacts(provenance, {now, minConfirmCount=3, recentDays=90, isInjection?})` (mirrors `selectPromotableMemories`): a fact earns DURABLE status iff NOT injection-flagged AND (`source==="user"` [user truth outranks inference, immediate] OR (`confirmCountвүҘ3` AND recent)). FAIL-CLOSE: an injection-flagged value is NEVER promoted however often confirmed; the `isInjection` check is dependency-injected (CLI passes the real `isMemoryInjection`) so @muse/memory stays agent-core-free. Pure (selects, never promotes-in-place вҖ” no partial side-effects). Wired into `muse memory why <key>` ("В· durable" / "В· provisional"). OUTCOME-verified (5 gate cases + the end-to-end fail-close via the wired detector) + Opus в‘Јb judge PASS 6/6. Consumes G3's `deriveFactProvenance`.
- вң“ (G4-followup) **Tie durable-vs-provisional to GROUNDING** вҖ” DONE (competitor-grounding fire 14, memory-integrity + grounding-floor). So a once-seen auto-extract (possible mis-extraction) is grounded cautiously, not asserted as confirmed (GROUNDED != TRUE on the source side). OUTCOME-verified end-to-end (log вҶ’ provisional вҶ’ annotated block; injection value marked AND defanged = defense-in-depth) + Opus в‘Јb judge PASS 7/7. (Honest scope: deterministic marking + prompt signal вҖ” not a claim the 8B fully obeys the tag.)

Verified genuinely-unbuilt (chat-repl.ts has ZERO decompose refs), BUT a POOR FIT: chat is a STREAMING continuous-companion REPL; `runDecomposedAgentAsk` is a non-streaming BATCH (N subtask runs + 1 synthesis, sequential on one GPU) вҶ’ bolting it in = a multi-second silent mid-conversation stall = UX regression on the exact surface built for liveness. ### Refill batch 2 (gap-scout fire 15, codegraph-verified open; G1-G6 + follow-ups all вң“)

- вң“ (H1-followup) auto re-synthesis вҖ” core-hardening fire 5 (orchestration): `runLeadWorkerTask` now does ONE verifier-gated re-synthesis when the first synthesis drops a sub-result. Registered in `scripts/reflection-guard.test.mjs` (external verifier = `verifySynthesisCoverage`, arXiv 2510.18254). - вң“ (H2) **Value-volatility signal in the durable-promotion gate** вҖ” DONE (competitor-grounding fire 16, memory-integrity; fixes a flaw in the builder's OWN fire-12 gate). `FactProvenance` gains `distinctValueCount` (`deriveFactProvenance`: `new Set(group.map(e=>e.value.trim())).size`). `selectPromotableFacts`' AUTO branch now requires `distinctValueCount === 1` (stable) on top of confirmCountвүҘ3 + recent вҖ” so a belief the auto-extractor gave CONFLICTING values for (address XвҶ’YвҶ’Z, distinctValueCount 3) no longer auto-promotes as durable (it was the INVERSE signal: re-confirmation of a CHANGING belief). A USER-stated fact still promotes regardless of flips (latest = their truth). The provisional chain is AUTOMATIC (volatile вҶ’ not durable вҶ’ `provisionalFactKeys` вҶ’ "(unconfirmed)" in grounding, fire 14). `muse memory why` shows "value changed NГ— (volatile)". OUTCOME-verified + Opus в‘Јb judge PASS 5/5 (the chosen distinctValueCount metric is MORE conservative/fail-safe than a current-value-run alternative, which would auto-promote a previously-contradicted value вҖ” riskier for the grounding floor). UNBLOCKS H4.
- в—‘ (H3) **Cross-lingual source-conflict detection** вҖ” Hangul-labelled subset DONE (competitor-grounding fire 18 = JUDGE-DRILL, grounding-floor). `LABELLED_VALUE` was `[A-Za-z]`-only вҶ’ a Hangul-labelled field ("мЈјмҶҢ: м„ңмҡё" vs "мЈјмҶҢ: л¶ҖмӮ°") never parsed and a Korean source-conflict was silently missed. ### Refill batch 3 (gap-scout fires 19-37)
- вң“ (Z1) **Thread a TRUNCATION partiality notice into the synthesis prompt (close a fan-out GROUNDEDвү TRUE leak) + JUDGE-DRILL** вҖ” competitor-grounding fire 37 (orchestration). When the lead-worker fan-out truncates the sub-task list to MAX_SUBTASKS (8), the dropped items never execute (not in `executions`, so `verifySynthesisCoverage` can't flag them). Before this fix, the synthesis prompt was identical to the untruncated path вҖ” the model presented the 8 survivors as a COMPLETE answer to an N-item (e.g. 11) request: a GROUNDEDвү TRUE leak in the answer TEXT (the channel the user reads), the MAST "unaware of termination" failure for truncation-dropped subtasks. FIX: `truncatedSynthesisRequest(request, dropped)` appends an explicit partiality directive (`[л¶Җл¶„ мқ‘лӢө вҖ” вҖҰ${dropped}к°ңк°Җ мІҳлҰ¬лҗҳм§Җ м•Ҡм•ҳлӢӨвҖҰлҲ„лқҪмқҙ мһҲмқҢмқ„ л°ҳл“ңмӢң лӘ…мӢңн•ҳлқј]`, mirrors the sibling `reinforceSynthesisRequest`); first synthesis + the re-synthesis retry base both carry it when truncated (sibling). ask-decompose `buildSynthesisPrompt` already embeds the engine-supplied request, so it reaches the model. - вң“ (Y1) **Scope the session-end playbook reward loop to INJECTABLE strategies (no fabricated reward attribution)** вҖ” competitor-grounding fire 36 (self-development).
